  3686 void
  3687 pgtk_clear_frame (struct frame *f)
  3688 {
  3689   if (!FRAME_DEFAULT_FACE (f))
  3690     return;
  3691 
  3692   mark_window_cursors_off (XWINDOW (FRAME_ROOT_WINDOW (f)));
  3693 
  3694   block_input ();
  3695   pgtk_clear_area (f, 0, 0, FRAME_PIXEL_WIDTH (f), FRAME_PIXEL_HEIGHT (f));
  3696   unblock_input ();
  3697 }
  3698 
  3699 static void
  3700 recover_from_visible_bell (struct atimer *timer)
  3701 {
  3702   struct frame *f = timer->client_data;
  3703 
  3704   if (FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->cr_surface_visible_bell != NULL)
  3705     {
  3706       cairo_surface_destroy (FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->cr_surface_visible_bell);
  3707       FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->cr_surface_visible_bell = NULL;
  3708     }
  3709 
  3710   if (FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->atimer_visible_bell != NULL)
  3711     FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->atimer_visible_bell = NULL;
  3712 }
  3713 
  3714 /* Invert the middle quarter of the frame for .15 sec.  */
  3715 
  3716 static void
  3717 pgtk_flash (struct frame *f)
  3718 {
  3719   cairo_surface_t *surface_orig, *surface;
  3720   cairo_t *cr;
  3721   int width, height, flash_height, flash_left, flash_right;
  3722   struct timespec delay;
  3723 
  3724   if (!FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f))
  3725     return;
  3726 
  3727   block_input ();
  3728 
  3729   surface_orig = FRAME_CR_SURFACE (f);
  3730 
  3731   width = FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_WIDTH (f);
  3732   height = FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_HEIGHT (f);
  3733   surface = cairo_surface_create_similar (surface_orig,
  3734                                           CAIRO_CONTENT_COLOR_ALPHA,
  3735                                           width, height);
  3736 
  3737   cr = cairo_create (surface);
  3738   cairo_set_source_surface (cr, surface_orig, 0, 0);
  3739   cairo_rectangle (cr, 0, 0, width, height);
  3740   cairo_clip (cr);
  3741   cairo_paint (cr);
  3742 
  3743   cairo_set_source_rgb (cr, 1, 1, 1);
  3744   cairo_set_operator (cr, CAIRO_OPERATOR_DIFFERENCE);
  3745 
  3746   /* Get the height not including a menu bar widget.  */
  3747   height = FRAME_PIXEL_HEIGHT (f);
  3748   /* Height of each line to flash.  */
  3749   flash_height = FRAME_LINE_HEIGHT (f);
  3750   /* These will be the left and right margins of the rectangles.  */
  3751   flash_left = FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f);
  3752   flash_right = (FRAME_PIXEL_WIDTH (f)
  3753                  - FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f));
  3754   width = flash_right - flash_left;
  3755 
  3756   /* If window is tall, flash top and bottom line.  */
  3757   if (height > 3 * FRAME_LINE_HEIGHT (f))
  3758     {
  3759       cairo_rectangle (cr,
  3760                        flash_left,
  3761                        (FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f)
  3762                         + FRAME_TOP_MARGIN_HEIGHT (f)),
  3763                        width, flash_height);
  3764       cairo_fill (cr);
  3765 
  3766       cairo_rectangle (cr,
  3767                        flash_left,
  3768                        (height - flash_height
  3769                         - FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f)),
  3770                        width, flash_height);
  3771       cairo_fill (cr);
  3772     }
  3773   else
  3774     {
  3775       /* If it is short, flash it all.  */
  3776       cairo_rectangle (cr,
  3777                        flash_left, FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f),
  3778                        width, height - 2 * FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f));
  3779       cairo_fill (cr);
  3780     }
  3781 
  3782   FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->cr_surface_visible_bell = surface;
  3783 
  3784   delay = make_timespec (0, 50 * 1000 * 1000);
  3785 
  3786   if (FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->atimer_visible_bell != NULL)
  3787     {
  3788       cancel_atimer (FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->atimer_visible_bell);
  3789       FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->atimer_visible_bell = NULL;
  3790     }
  3791 
  3792   FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->atimer_visible_bell
  3793     = start_atimer (ATIMER_RELATIVE, delay, recover_from_visible_bell, f);
  3794 
  3795 
  3796   cairo_destroy (cr);
  3797   unblock_input ();
  3798 }
  3799 
  3800 /* Make audible bell.  */
  3801 
  3802 static void
  3803 pgtk_ring_bell (struct frame *f)
  3804 {
  3805   if (visible_bell)
  3806     {
  3807       pgtk_flash (f);
  3808     }
  3809   else
  3810     {
  3811       block_input ();
  3812       gtk_widget_error_bell (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f));
  3813       unblock_input ();
  3814     }
  3815 }
  3816 
  3817 /* Read events coming from the X server.
  3818    Return as soon as there are no more events to be read.
  3819 
  3820    Return the number of characters stored into the buffer,
  3821    thus pretending to be `read' (except the characters we store
  3822    in the keyboard buffer can be multibyte, so are not necessarily
  3823    C chars).  */
  3824 
  3825 static int
  3826 pgtk_read_socket (struct terminal *terminal, struct input_event *hold_quit)
  3827 {
  3828   GMainContext *context;
  3829   bool context_acquired = false;
  3830   int count;
  3831 
  3832   count = evq_flush (hold_quit);
  3833   if (count > 0)
  3834     {
  3835       return count;
  3836     }
  3837 
  3838   context = g_main_context_default ();
  3839   context_acquired = g_main_context_acquire (context);
  3840 
  3841   block_input ();
  3842 
  3843   if (context_acquired)
  3844     {
  3845       while (g_main_context_pending (context))
  3846         {
  3847           g_main_context_dispatch (context);
  3848         }
  3849     }
  3850 
  3851   unblock_input ();
  3852 
  3853   if (context_acquired)
  3854     g_main_context_release (context);
  3855 
  3856   count = evq_flush (hold_quit);
  3857   if (count > 0)
  3858     {
  3859       return count;
  3860     }
  3861 
  3862   return 0;
  3863 }
  3864 
  3865 /* Lisp window being scrolled.  Set when starting to interact with
  3866    a toolkit scroll bar, reset to nil when ending the interaction.  */
  3867 
  3868 static Lisp_Object window_being_scrolled;
  3869 
  3870 static void
  3871 pgtk_send_scroll_bar_event (Lisp_Object window, enum scroll_bar_part part,
  3872                             int portion, int whole, bool horizontal)
  3873 {
  3874   union buffered_input_event inev;
  3875 
  3876   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  3877 
  3878   inev.ie.kind = (horizontal
  3879                   ? HORIZONTAL_SCROLL_BAR_CLICK_EVENT
  3880                   : SCROLL_BAR_CLICK_EVENT);
  3881   inev.ie.frame_or_window = window;
  3882   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  3883   inev.ie.timestamp = 0;
  3884   inev.ie.code = 0;
  3885   inev.ie.part = part;
  3886   inev.ie.x = make_fixnum (portion);
  3887   inev.ie.y = make_fixnum (whole);
  3888   inev.ie.modifiers = 0;
  3889 
  3890   evq_enqueue (&inev);
  3891 }
  3892 
  3893 
  3894 /* Scroll bar callback for GTK scroll bars.  WIDGET is the scroll
  3895    bar widget.  DATA is a pointer to the scroll_bar structure. */
  3896 
  3897 static gboolean
  3898 xg_scroll_callback (GtkRange * range,
  3899                     GtkScrollType scroll, gdouble value, gpointer user_data)
  3900 {
  3901   int whole = 0, portion = 0;
  3902   struct scroll_bar *bar = user_data;
  3903   enum scroll_bar_part part = scroll_bar_nowhere;
  3904   GtkAdjustment *adj = GTK_ADJUSTMENT (gtk_range_get_adjustment (range));
  3905 
  3906   if (xg_ignore_gtk_scrollbar)
  3907     return false;
  3908 
  3909   switch (scroll)
  3910     {
  3911     case GTK_SCROLL_JUMP:
  3912       if (bar->horizontal)
  3913         {
  3914           part = scroll_bar_horizontal_handle;
  3915           whole = (int) (gtk_adjustment_get_upper (adj) -
  3916                          gtk_adjustment_get_page_size (adj));
  3917           portion = min ((int) value, whole);
  3918           bar->dragging = portion;
  3919         }
  3920       else
  3921         {
  3922           part = scroll_bar_handle;
  3923           whole = gtk_adjustment_get_upper (adj) -
  3924             gtk_adjustment_get_page_size (adj);
  3925           portion = min ((int) value, whole);
  3926           bar->dragging = portion;
  3927         }
  3928       break;
  3929     case GTK_SCROLL_STEP_BACKWARD:
  3930       part = (bar->horizontal ? scroll_bar_left_arrow : scroll_bar_up_arrow);
  3931       bar->dragging = -1;
  3932       break;
  3933     case GTK_SCROLL_STEP_FORWARD:
  3934       part = (bar->horizontal
  3935               ? scroll_bar_right_arrow : scroll_bar_down_arrow);
  3936       bar->dragging = -1;
  3937       break;
  3938     case GTK_SCROLL_PAGE_BACKWARD:
  3939       part = (bar->horizontal
  3940               ? scroll_bar_before_handle : scroll_bar_above_handle);
  3941       bar->dragging = -1;
  3942       break;
  3943     case GTK_SCROLL_PAGE_FORWARD:
  3944       part = (bar->horizontal
  3945               ? scroll_bar_after_handle : scroll_bar_below_handle);
  3946       bar->dragging = -1;
  3947       break;
  3948     default:
  3949       break;
  3950     }
  3951 
  3952   if (part != scroll_bar_nowhere)
  3953     {
  3954       window_being_scrolled = bar->window;
  3955       pgtk_send_scroll_bar_event (bar->window, part, portion, whole,
  3956                                   bar->horizontal);
  3957     }
  3958 
  3959   return false;
  3960 }
  3961 
  3962 /* Callback for button release. Sets dragging to -1 when dragging is done.  */
  3963 
  3964 static gboolean
  3965 xg_end_scroll_callback (GtkWidget * widget,
  3966                         GdkEventButton * event, gpointer user_data)
  3967 {
  3968   struct scroll_bar *bar = user_data;
  3969   bar->dragging = -1;
  3970   if (WINDOWP (window_being_scrolled))
  3971     {
  3972       pgtk_send_scroll_bar_event (window_being_scrolled,
  3973                                   scroll_bar_end_scroll, 0, 0,
  3974                                   bar->horizontal);
  3975       window_being_scrolled = Qnil;
  3976     }
  3977 
  3978   return false;
  3979 }
  3980 
  3981 #define SCROLL_BAR_NAME "verticalScrollBar"
  3982 #define SCROLL_BAR_HORIZONTAL_NAME "horizontalScrollBar"
  3983 
  3984 /* Create the widget for scroll bar BAR on frame F.  Record the widget
  3985    and X window of the scroll bar in BAR.  */
  3986 
  3987 static void
  3988 pgtk_create_toolkit_scroll_bar (struct frame *f, struct scroll_bar *bar)
  3989 {
  3990   const char *scroll_bar_name = SCROLL_BAR_NAME;
  3991 
  3992   block_input ();
  3993   xg_create_scroll_bar (f, bar, G_CALLBACK (xg_scroll_callback),
  3994                         G_CALLBACK (xg_end_scroll_callback), scroll_bar_name);
  3995   unblock_input ();
  3996 }
  3997 
  3998 static void
  3999 pgtk_create_horizontal_toolkit_scroll_bar (struct frame *f,
  4000                                            struct scroll_bar *bar)
  4001 {
  4002   const char *scroll_bar_name = SCROLL_BAR_HORIZONTAL_NAME;
  4003 
  4004   block_input ();
  4005   xg_create_horizontal_scroll_bar (f, bar, G_CALLBACK (xg_scroll_callback),
  4006                                    G_CALLBACK (xg_end_scroll_callback),
  4007                                    scroll_bar_name);
  4008   unblock_input ();
  4009 }
  4010 
  4011 /* Set the thumb size and position of scroll bar BAR.  We are currently
  4012    displaying PORTION out of a whole WHOLE, and our position POSITION.  */
  4013 
  4014 static void
  4015 pgtk_set_toolkit_scroll_bar_thumb (struct scroll_bar *bar, int portion,
  4016                                    int position, int whole)
  4017 {
  4018   xg_set_toolkit_scroll_bar_thumb (bar, portion, position, whole);
  4019 }
  4020 
  4021 static void
  4022 pgtk_set_toolkit_horizontal_scroll_bar_thumb (struct scroll_bar *bar,
  4023                                               int portion, int position,
  4024                                               int whole)
  4025 {
  4026   xg_set_toolkit_horizontal_scroll_bar_thumb (bar, portion, position, whole);
  4027 }
  4028 
  4029 /* Create a scroll bar and return the scroll bar vector for it.  W is
  4030    the Emacs window on which to create the scroll bar. TOP, LEFT,
  4031    WIDTH and HEIGHT are the pixel coordinates and dimensions of the
  4032    scroll bar. */
  4033 
  4034 static struct scroll_bar *
  4035 pgtk_scroll_bar_create (struct window *w, int top, int left,
  4036                         int width, int height, bool horizontal)
  4037 {
  4038   struct frame *f = XFRAME (w->frame);
  4039   struct scroll_bar *bar
  4040     = ALLOCATE_PSEUDOVECTOR (struct scroll_bar, prev, PVEC_OTHER);
  4041   Lisp_Object barobj;
  4042 
  4043   block_input ();
  4044 
  4045   if (horizontal)
  4046     pgtk_create_horizontal_toolkit_scroll_bar (f, bar);
  4047   else
  4048     pgtk_create_toolkit_scroll_bar (f, bar);
  4049 
  4050   XSETWINDOW (bar->window, w);
  4051   bar->top = top;
  4052   bar->left = left;
  4053   bar->width = width;
  4054   bar->height = height;
  4055   bar->start = 0;
  4056   bar->end = 0;
  4057   bar->dragging = -1;
  4058   bar->horizontal = horizontal;
  4059 
  4060   /* Add bar to its frame's list of scroll bars.  */
  4061   bar->next = FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (f);
  4062   bar->prev = Qnil;
  4063   XSETVECTOR (barobj, bar);
  4064   fset_scroll_bars (f, barobj);
  4065   if (!NILP (bar->next))
  4066     XSETVECTOR (XSCROLL_BAR (bar->next)->prev, bar);
  4067 
  4068   /* Map the window/widget.  */
  4069   {
  4070     if (horizontal)
  4071       xg_update_horizontal_scrollbar_pos (f, bar->x_window, top,
  4072                                           left, width, max (height, 1));
  4073     else
  4074       xg_update_scrollbar_pos (f, bar->x_window, top,
  4075                                left, width, max (height, 1));
  4076   }
  4077 
  4078   unblock_input ();
  4079   return bar;
  4080 }
  4081 
  4082 /* Destroy scroll bar BAR, and set its Emacs window's scroll bar to
  4083    nil.  */
  4084 
  4085 static void
  4086 pgtk_scroll_bar_remove (struct scroll_bar *bar)
  4087 {
  4088   struct frame *f = XFRAME (WINDOW_FRAME (XWINDOW (bar->window)));
  4089   block_input ();
  4090 
  4091   xg_remove_scroll_bar (f, bar->x_window);
  4092 
  4093   /* Dissociate this scroll bar from its window.  */
  4094   if (bar->horizontal)
  4095     wset_horizontal_scroll_bar (XWINDOW (bar->window), Qnil);
  4096   else
  4097     wset_vertical_scroll_bar (XWINDOW (bar->window), Qnil);
  4098 
  4099   unblock_input ();
  4100 }
  4101 
  4102 /* Set the handle of the vertical scroll bar for WINDOW to indicate
  4103    that we are displaying PORTION characters out of a total of WHOLE
  4104    characters, starting at POSITION.  If WINDOW has no scroll bar,
  4105    create one.  */
  4106 
  4107 static void
  4108 pgtk_set_vertical_scroll_bar (struct window *w, int portion, int whole,
  4109                               int position)
  4110 {
  4111   struct frame *f = XFRAME (w->frame);
  4112   Lisp_Object barobj;
  4113   struct scroll_bar *bar;
  4114   int top, height, left, width;
  4115   int window_y, window_height;
  4116 
  4117   /* Get window dimensions.  */
  4118   window_box (w, ANY_AREA, 0, &window_y, 0, &window_height);
  4119   top = window_y;
  4120   height = window_height;
  4121   left = WINDOW_SCROLL_BAR_AREA_X (w);
  4122   width = WINDOW_SCROLL_BAR_AREA_WIDTH (w);
  4123 
  4124   /* Does the scroll bar exist yet?  */
  4125   if (NILP (w->vertical_scroll_bar))
  4126     {
  4127       if (width > 0 && height > 0)
  4128         {
  4129           block_input ();
  4130           pgtk_clear_area (f, left, top, width, height);
  4131           unblock_input ();
  4132         }
  4133 
  4134       bar = pgtk_scroll_bar_create (w, top, left, width, max (height, 1), false);
  4135     }
  4136   else
  4137     {
  4138       /* It may just need to be moved and resized.  */
  4139       unsigned int mask = 0;
  4140 
  4141       bar = XSCROLL_BAR (w->vertical_scroll_bar);
  4142 
  4143       block_input ();
  4144 
  4145       if (left != bar->left)
  4146         mask |= 1;
  4147       if (top != bar->top)
  4148         mask |= 1;
  4149       if (width != bar->width)
  4150         mask |= 1;
  4151       if (height != bar->height)
  4152         mask |= 1;
  4153 
  4154       /* Move/size the scroll bar widget.  */
  4155       if (mask)
  4156         {
  4157           /* Since toolkit scroll bars are smaller than the space reserved
  4158              for them on the frame, we have to clear "under" them.  */
  4159           if (width > 0 && height > 0)
  4160             pgtk_clear_area (f, left, top, width, height);
  4161           xg_update_scrollbar_pos (f, bar->x_window, top,
  4162                                    left, width, max (height, 1));
  4163         }
  4164 
  4165       /* Remember new settings.  */
  4166       bar->left = left;
  4167       bar->top = top;
  4168       bar->width = width;
  4169       bar->height = height;
  4170 
  4171       unblock_input ();
  4172     }
  4173 
  4174   pgtk_set_toolkit_scroll_bar_thumb (bar, portion, position, whole);
  4175 
  4176   XSETVECTOR (barobj, bar);
  4177   wset_vertical_scroll_bar (w, barobj);
  4178 }
  4179 
  4180 static void
  4181 pgtk_set_horizontal_scroll_bar (struct window *w, int portion, int whole,
  4182                                 int position)
  4183 {
  4184   struct frame *f = XFRAME (w->frame);
  4185   Lisp_Object barobj;
  4186   struct scroll_bar *bar;
  4187   int top, height, left, width;
  4188   int window_x, window_width;
  4189   int pixel_width = WINDOW_PIXEL_WIDTH (w);
  4190 
  4191   /* Get window dimensions.  */
  4192   window_box (w, ANY_AREA, &window_x, 0, &window_width, 0);
  4193   left = window_x;
  4194   width = window_width;
  4195   top = WINDOW_SCROLL_BAR_AREA_Y (w);
  4196   height = WINDOW_SCROLL_BAR_AREA_HEIGHT (w);
  4197 
  4198   /* Does the scroll bar exist yet?  */
  4199   if (NILP (w->horizontal_scroll_bar))
  4200     {
  4201       if (width > 0 && height > 0)
  4202         {
  4203           block_input ();
  4204 
  4205           /* Clear also part between window_width and
  4206              WINDOW_PIXEL_WIDTH.  */
  4207           pgtk_clear_area (f, left, top, pixel_width, height);
  4208           unblock_input ();
  4209         }
  4210 
  4211       bar = pgtk_scroll_bar_create (w, top, left, width, height, true);
  4212     }
  4213   else
  4214     {
  4215       /* It may just need to be moved and resized.  */
  4216       unsigned int mask = 0;
  4217 
  4218       bar = XSCROLL_BAR (w->horizontal_scroll_bar);
  4219 
  4220       block_input ();
  4221 
  4222       if (left != bar->left)
  4223         mask |= 1;
  4224       if (top != bar->top)
  4225         mask |= 1;
  4226       if (width != bar->width)
  4227         mask |= 1;
  4228       if (height != bar->height)
  4229         mask |= 1;
  4230 
  4231       /* Move/size the scroll bar widget.  */
  4232       if (mask)
  4233         {
  4234           /* Since toolkit scroll bars are smaller than the space reserved
  4235              for them on the frame, we have to clear "under" them.  */
  4236           if (width > 0 && height > 0)
  4237             pgtk_clear_area (f,
  4238                              WINDOW_LEFT_EDGE_X (w), top,
  4239                              pixel_width - WINDOW_RIGHT_DIVIDER_WIDTH (w),
  4240                              height);
  4241           xg_update_horizontal_scrollbar_pos (f, bar->x_window, top, left,
  4242                                               width, height);
  4243         }
  4244 
  4245       /* Remember new settings.  */
  4246       bar->left = left;
  4247       bar->top = top;
  4248       bar->width = width;
  4249       bar->height = height;
  4250 
  4251       unblock_input ();
  4252     }
  4253 
  4254   pgtk_set_toolkit_horizontal_scroll_bar_thumb (bar, portion, position, whole);
  4255 
  4256   XSETVECTOR (barobj, bar);
  4257   wset_horizontal_scroll_bar (w, barobj);
  4258 }
  4259 
  4260 /* The following three hooks are used when we're doing a thorough
  4261    redisplay of the frame.  We don't explicitly know which scroll bars
  4262    are going to be deleted, because keeping track of when windows go
  4263    away is a real pain - "Can you say set-window-configuration, boys
  4264    and girls?"  Instead, we just assert at the beginning of redisplay
  4265    that *all* scroll bars are to be removed, and then save a scroll bar
  4266    from the fiery pit when we actually redisplay its window.  */
  4267 
  4268 /* Arrange for all scroll bars on FRAME to be removed at the next call
  4269    to `*judge_scroll_bars_hook'.  A scroll bar may be spared if
  4270    `*redeem_scroll_bar_hook' is applied to its window before the judgment.  */
  4271 
  4272 static void
  4273 pgtk_condemn_scroll_bars (struct frame *frame)
  4274 {
  4275   if (!NILP (FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (frame)))
  4276     {
  4277       if (!NILP (FRAME_CONDEMNED_SCROLL_BARS (frame)))
  4278         {
  4279           /* Prepend scrollbars to already condemned ones.  */
  4280           Lisp_Object last = FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (frame);
  4281 
  4282           while (!NILP (XSCROLL_BAR (last)->next))
  4283             last = XSCROLL_BAR (last)->next;
  4284 
  4285           XSCROLL_BAR (last)->next = FRAME_CONDEMNED_SCROLL_BARS (frame);
  4286           XSCROLL_BAR (FRAME_CONDEMNED_SCROLL_BARS (frame))->prev = last;
  4287         }
  4288 
  4289       fset_condemned_scroll_bars (frame, FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (frame));
  4290       fset_scroll_bars (frame, Qnil);
  4291     }
  4292 }
  4293 
  4294 /* Un-mark WINDOW's scroll bar for deletion in this judgment cycle.
  4295    Note that WINDOW isn't necessarily condemned at all.  */
  4296 
  4297 static void
  4298 pgtk_redeem_scroll_bar (struct window *w)
  4299 {
  4300   struct scroll_bar *bar;
  4301   Lisp_Object barobj;
  4302   struct frame *f;
  4303 
  4304   /* We can't redeem this window's scroll bar if it doesn't have one.  */
  4305   if (NILP (w->vertical_scroll_bar) && NILP (w->horizontal_scroll_bar))
  4306     emacs_abort ();
  4307 
  4308   if (!NILP (w->vertical_scroll_bar) && WINDOW_HAS_VERTICAL_SCROLL_BAR (w))
  4309     {
  4310       bar = XSCROLL_BAR (w->vertical_scroll_bar);
  4311       /* Unlink it from the condemned list.  */
  4312       f = XFRAME (WINDOW_FRAME (w));
  4313       if (NILP (bar->prev))
  4314         {
  4315           /* If the prev pointer is nil, it must be the first in one of
  4316              the lists.  */
  4317           if (EQ (FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (f), w->vertical_scroll_bar))
  4318             /* It's not condemned.  Everything's fine.  */
  4319             goto horizontal;
  4320           else if (EQ (FRAME_CONDEMNED_SCROLL_BARS (f),
  4321                        w->vertical_scroll_bar))
  4322             fset_condemned_scroll_bars (f, bar->next);
  4323           else
  4324             /* If its prev pointer is nil, it must be at the front of
  4325                one or the other!  */
  4326             emacs_abort ();
  4327         }
  4328       else
  4329         XSCROLL_BAR (bar->prev)->next = bar->next;
  4330 
  4331       if (!NILP (bar->next))
  4332         XSCROLL_BAR (bar->next)->prev = bar->prev;
  4333 
  4334       bar->next = FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (f);
  4335       bar->prev = Qnil;
  4336       XSETVECTOR (barobj, bar);
  4337       fset_scroll_bars (f, barobj);
  4338       if (!NILP (bar->next))
  4339         XSETVECTOR (XSCROLL_BAR (bar->next)->prev, bar);
  4340     }
  4341 
  4342 horizontal:
  4343   if (!NILP (w->horizontal_scroll_bar)
  4344       && WINDOW_HAS_HORIZONTAL_SCROLL_BAR (w))
  4345     {
  4346       bar = XSCROLL_BAR (w->horizontal_scroll_bar);
  4347       /* Unlink it from the condemned list.  */
  4348       f = XFRAME (WINDOW_FRAME (w));
  4349       if (NILP (bar->prev))
  4350         {
  4351           /* If the prev pointer is nil, it must be the first in one of
  4352              the lists.  */
  4353           if (EQ (FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (f), w->horizontal_scroll_bar))
  4354             /* It's not condemned.  Everything's fine.  */
  4355             return;
  4356           else if (EQ (FRAME_CONDEMNED_SCROLL_BARS (f),
  4357                        w->horizontal_scroll_bar))
  4358             fset_condemned_scroll_bars (f, bar->next);
  4359           else
  4360             /* If its prev pointer is nil, it must be at the front of
  4361                one or the other!  */
  4362             emacs_abort ();
  4363         }
  4364       else
  4365         XSCROLL_BAR (bar->prev)->next = bar->next;
  4366 
  4367       if (!NILP (bar->next))
  4368         XSCROLL_BAR (bar->next)->prev = bar->prev;
  4369 
  4370       bar->next = FRAME_SCROLL_BARS (f);
  4371       bar->prev = Qnil;
  4372       XSETVECTOR (barobj, bar);
  4373       fset_scroll_bars (f, barobj);
  4374       if (!NILP (bar->next))
  4375         XSETVECTOR (XSCROLL_BAR (bar->next)->prev, bar);
  4376     }
  4377 }
  4378 
  4379 /* Remove all scroll bars on FRAME that haven't been saved since the
  4380    last call to `*condemn_scroll_bars_hook'.  */
  4381 
  4382 static void
  4383 pgtk_judge_scroll_bars (struct frame *f)
  4384 {
  4385   Lisp_Object bar, next;
  4386 
  4387   bar = FRAME_CONDEMNED_SCROLL_BARS (f);
  4388 
  4389   /* Clear out the condemned list now so we won't try to process any
  4390      more events on the hapless scroll bars.  */
  4391   fset_condemned_scroll_bars (f, Qnil);
  4392 
  4393   for (; !NILP (bar); bar = next)
  4394     {
  4395       struct scroll_bar *b = XSCROLL_BAR (bar);
  4396 
  4397       pgtk_scroll_bar_remove (b);
  4398 
  4399       next = b->next;
  4400       b->next = b->prev = Qnil;
  4401     }
  4402 
  4403   /* Now there should be no references to the condemned scroll bars,
  4404      and they should get garbage-collected.  */
  4405 }
  4406 
  4407 static void
  4408 set_fullscreen_state (struct frame *f)
  4409 {
  4410   if (!FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f))
  4411     return;
  4412 
  4413   GtkWindow *widget = GTK_WINDOW (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f));
  4414   switch (f->want_fullscreen)
  4415     {
  4416     case FULLSCREEN_NONE:
  4417       gtk_window_unfullscreen (widget);
  4418       gtk_window_unmaximize (widget);
  4419       store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qnil);
  4420       break;
  4421 
  4422     case FULLSCREEN_BOTH:
  4423       gtk_window_unmaximize (widget);
  4424       gtk_window_fullscreen (widget);
  4425       store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qfullboth);
  4426       break;
  4427 
  4428     case FULLSCREEN_MAXIMIZED:
  4429       gtk_window_unfullscreen (widget);
  4430       gtk_window_maximize (widget);
  4431       store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qmaximized);
  4432       break;
  4433 
  4434     case FULLSCREEN_WIDTH:
  4435     case FULLSCREEN_HEIGHT:
  4436       /* Not supported by gtk. Ignore them. */
  4437       break;
  4438     }
  4439 
  4440   f->want_fullscreen = FULLSCREEN_NONE;
  4441 }
  4442 
  4443 static void
  4444 pgtk_fullscreen_hook (struct frame *f)
  4445 {
  4446   if (FRAME_VISIBLE_P (f))
  4447     {
  4448       block_input ();
  4449       set_fullscreen_state (f);
  4450       unblock_input ();
  4451     }
  4452 }
  4453 
  4454 /* This function is called when the last frame on a display is deleted. */
  4455 void
  4456 pgtk_delete_terminal (struct terminal *terminal)
  4457 {
  4458   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo = terminal->display_info.pgtk;
  4459 
  4460   /* Protect against recursive calls.  delete_frame in
  4461      delete_terminal calls us back when it deletes our last frame.  */
  4462   if (!terminal->name)
  4463     return;
  4464 
  4465   block_input ();
  4466 
  4467   pgtk_im_finish (dpyinfo);
  4468 
  4469   /* Normally, the display is available...  */
  4470   if (dpyinfo->gdpy)
  4471     {
  4472       image_destroy_all_bitmaps (dpyinfo);
  4473 
  4474       g_clear_object (&dpyinfo->xg_cursor);
  4475       g_clear_object (&dpyinfo->vertical_scroll_bar_cursor);
  4476       g_clear_object (&dpyinfo->horizontal_scroll_bar_cursor);
  4477       g_clear_object (&dpyinfo->invisible_cursor);
  4478       if (dpyinfo->last_click_event != NULL)
  4479         {
  4480           gdk_event_free (dpyinfo->last_click_event);
  4481           dpyinfo->last_click_event = NULL;
  4482         }
  4483 
  4484       /* Disconnect these handlers before the display closes so
  4485          useless removal signals don't fire.  */
  4486       g_signal_handlers_disconnect_by_func (G_OBJECT (dpyinfo->gdpy),
  4487                                             G_CALLBACK (pgtk_seat_added_cb),
  4488                                             dpyinfo);
  4489       g_signal_handlers_disconnect_by_func (G_OBJECT (dpyinfo->gdpy),
  4490                                             G_CALLBACK (pgtk_seat_removed_cb),
  4491                                             dpyinfo);
  4492       xg_display_close (dpyinfo->gdpy);
  4493 
  4494       dpyinfo->gdpy = NULL;
  4495     }
  4496 
  4497   if (dpyinfo->connection >= 0)
  4498     emacs_close (dpyinfo->connection);
  4499 
  4500   dpyinfo->connection = -1;
  4501 
  4502   delete_keyboard_wait_descriptor (0);
  4503 
  4504   pgtk_delete_display (dpyinfo);
  4505   unblock_input ();
  4506 }
  4507 
  4508 /* Store F's background color into *BGCOLOR.  */
  4509 static void
  4510 pgtk_query_frame_background_color (struct frame *f, Emacs_Color * bgcolor)
  4511 {
  4512   bgcolor->pixel = FRAME_BACKGROUND_PIXEL (f);
  4513   pgtk_query_color (f, bgcolor);
  4514 }

  4516 static void
  4517 pgtk_free_pixmap (struct frame *f, Emacs_Pixmap pixmap)
  4518 {
  4519   if (pixmap)
  4520     {
  4521       xfree (pixmap->data);
  4522       xfree (pixmap);
  4523     }
  4524 }
  4525 
  4526 void
  4527 pgtk_focus_frame (struct frame *f, bool noactivate)
  4528 {
  4529   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  4530   GtkWidget *widget;
  4531   GtkWindow *window;
  4532 
  4533   dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f);
  4534 
  4535   if (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f) && !noactivate)
  4536     {
  4537       /* The user says it is okay to activate the frame.  Call
  4538          gtk_window_present_with_time.  If the timestamp specified
  4539          (actually a display serial on Wayland) is new enough, then
  4540          any Wayland compositor supporting gtk_surface1_present will
  4541          cause the frame to be activated.  */
  4542 
  4543       window = GTK_WINDOW (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f));
  4544       gtk_window_present_with_time (window, dpyinfo->last_user_time);
  4545       return;
  4546     }
  4547 
  4548   widget = FRAME_WIDGET (f);
  4549 
  4550   if (widget)
  4551     gtk_widget_grab_focus (widget);
  4552 }
  4553 
  4554 static void
  4555 set_opacity_recursively (GtkWidget *w, gpointer data)
  4556 {
  4557   gtk_widget_set_opacity (w, *(double *) data);
  4558 
  4559   if (GTK_IS_CONTAINER (w))
  4560     gtk_container_foreach (GTK_CONTAINER (w),
  4561                            set_opacity_recursively, data);
  4562 }
  4563 
  4564 static void
  4565 pgtk_set_frame_alpha (struct frame *f)
  4566 {
  4567   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f);
  4568   double alpha = 1.0;
  4569   double alpha_min = 1.0;
  4570 
  4571   if (dpyinfo->highlight_frame == f)
  4572     alpha = f->alpha[0];
  4573   else
  4574     alpha = f->alpha[1];
  4575 
  4576   if (alpha < 0.0)
  4577     return;
  4578 
  4579   if (FLOATP (Vframe_alpha_lower_limit))
  4580     alpha_min = XFLOAT_DATA (Vframe_alpha_lower_limit);
  4581   else if (FIXNUMP (Vframe_alpha_lower_limit))
  4582     alpha_min = (XFIXNUM (Vframe_alpha_lower_limit)) / 100.0;
  4583 
  4584   if (alpha > 1.0)
  4585     alpha = 1.0;
  4586   else if (alpha < alpha_min && alpha_min <= 1.0)
  4587     alpha = alpha_min;
  4588 
  4589   set_opacity_recursively (FRAME_WIDGET (f), &alpha);
  4590   /* without this, blending mode is strange on wayland. */
  4591   gtk_widget_queue_resize_no_redraw (FRAME_WIDGET (f));
  4592 }
  4593 
  4594 static void
  4595 frame_highlight (struct frame *f)
  4596 {
  4597   block_input ();
  4598   GtkWidget *w = FRAME_WIDGET (f);
  4599 
  4600   char *css = g_strdup_printf ("decoration { border: solid %dpx #%06x; }",
  4601                                f->border_width,
  4602                                ((unsigned int) FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->border_pixel
  4603                                 & 0x00ffffff));
  4604 
  4605   GtkStyleContext *ctxt = gtk_widget_get_style_context (w);
  4606   GtkCssProvider *css_provider = gtk_css_provider_new ();
  4607   gtk_css_provider_load_from_data (css_provider, css, -1, NULL);
  4608   gtk_style_context_add_provider (ctxt, GTK_STYLE_PROVIDER (css_provider),
  4609                                   GTK_STYLE_PROVIDER_PRIORITY_USER);
  4610   g_free (css);
  4611 
  4612   GtkCssProvider *old = FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->border_color_css_provider;
  4613   FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->border_color_css_provider = css_provider;
  4614   if (old != NULL)
  4615     {
  4616       gtk_style_context_remove_provider (ctxt, GTK_STYLE_PROVIDER (old));
  4617       g_object_unref (old);
  4618     }
  4619 
  4620   unblock_input ();
  4621   gui_update_cursor (f, true);
  4622   pgtk_set_frame_alpha (f);
  4623 }
  4624 
  4625 static void
  4626 frame_unhighlight (struct frame *f)
  4627 {
  4628   GtkWidget *w;
  4629   char *css;
  4630   GtkStyleContext *ctxt;
  4631   GtkCssProvider *css_provider, *old;
  4632 
  4633   block_input ();
  4634 
  4635   w = FRAME_WIDGET (f);
  4636 
  4637   css = g_strdup_printf ("decoration { border: dotted %dpx #ffffff; }",
  4638                          f->border_width);
  4639 
  4640   ctxt = gtk_widget_get_style_context (w);
  4641   css_provider = gtk_css_provider_new ();
  4642   gtk_css_provider_load_from_data (css_provider, css, -1, NULL);
  4643   gtk_style_context_add_provider (ctxt, GTK_STYLE_PROVIDER (css_provider),
  4644                                   GTK_STYLE_PROVIDER_PRIORITY_USER);
  4645   g_free (css);
  4646 
  4647   old = FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->border_color_css_provider;
  4648   FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->border_color_css_provider = css_provider;
  4649   if (old != NULL)
  4650     {
  4651       gtk_style_context_remove_provider (ctxt, GTK_STYLE_PROVIDER (old));
  4652       g_object_unref (old);
  4653     }
  4654 
  4655   unblock_input ();
  4656   gui_update_cursor (f, true);
  4657   pgtk_set_frame_alpha (f);
  4658 }

  4660 
  4661 void
  4662 pgtk_frame_rehighlight (struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo)
  4663 {
  4664   struct frame *old_highlight = dpyinfo->highlight_frame;
  4665 
  4666   if (dpyinfo->x_focus_frame)
  4667     {
  4668       dpyinfo->highlight_frame
  4669         = ((FRAMEP (FRAME_FOCUS_FRAME (dpyinfo->x_focus_frame)))
  4670            ? XFRAME (FRAME_FOCUS_FRAME (dpyinfo->x_focus_frame))
  4671            : dpyinfo->x_focus_frame);
  4672       if (!FRAME_LIVE_P (dpyinfo->highlight_frame))
  4673         {
  4674           fset_focus_frame (dpyinfo->x_focus_frame, Qnil);
  4675           dpyinfo->highlight_frame = dpyinfo->x_focus_frame;
  4676         }
  4677     }
  4678   else
  4679     dpyinfo->highlight_frame = 0;
  4680 
  4681   if (old_highlight)
  4682     frame_unhighlight (old_highlight);
  4683   if (dpyinfo->highlight_frame)
  4684     frame_highlight (dpyinfo->highlight_frame);
  4685 }
  4686 
  4687 /* The focus has changed, or we have redirected a frame's focus to
  4688    another frame (this happens when a frame uses a surrogate
  4689    mini-buffer frame).  Shift the highlight as appropriate.
  4690 
  4691    The FRAME argument doesn't necessarily have anything to do with which
  4692    frame is being highlighted or un-highlighted; we only use it to find
  4693    the appropriate X display info.  */
  4694 
  4695 static void
  4696 pgtk_frame_rehighlight_hook (struct frame *frame)
  4697 {
  4698   pgtk_frame_rehighlight (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame));
  4699 }
  4700 
  4701 /* Set whether or not the mouse pointer should be visible on frame
  4702    F.  */
  4703 static void
  4704 pgtk_toggle_invisible_pointer (struct frame *f, bool invisible)
  4705 {
  4706   Emacs_Cursor cursor;
  4707   if (invisible)
  4708     cursor = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f)->invisible_cursor;
  4709   else
  4710     cursor = f->output_data.pgtk->current_cursor;
  4711   gdk_window_set_cursor (gtk_widget_get_window (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)),
  4712                          cursor);
  4713   f->pointer_invisible = invisible;
  4714 
  4715   /* This is needed to make the pointer visible upon receiving a
  4716      motion notify event.  */
  4717   gdk_display_flush (FRAME_X_DISPLAY (f));
  4718 }
  4719 
  4720 /* The focus has changed.  Update the frames as necessary to reflect
  4721    the new situation.  Note that we can't change the selected frame
  4722    here, because the Lisp code we are interrupting might become confused.
  4723    Each event gets marked with the frame in which it occurred, so the
  4724    Lisp code can tell when the switch took place by examining the events.  */
  4725 
  4726 static void
  4727 pgtk_new_focus_frame (struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo, struct frame *frame)
  4728 {
  4729   struct frame *old_focus = dpyinfo->x_focus_frame;
  4730   /* doesn't work on wayland */
  4731 
  4732   if (frame != dpyinfo->x_focus_frame)
  4733     {
  4734       /* Set this before calling other routines, so that they see
  4735          the correct value of x_focus_frame.  */
  4736       dpyinfo->x_focus_frame = frame;
  4737 
  4738       if (old_focus && old_focus->auto_lower)
  4739         if (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (old_focus))
  4740           gdk_window_lower (gtk_widget_get_window
  4741                             (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (old_focus)));
  4742 
  4743       if (dpyinfo->x_focus_frame && dpyinfo->x_focus_frame->auto_raise)
  4744         if (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (dpyinfo->x_focus_frame))
  4745           gdk_window_raise (gtk_widget_get_window
  4746                             (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (dpyinfo->x_focus_frame)));
  4747     }
  4748 
  4749   pgtk_frame_rehighlight (dpyinfo);
  4750 }
  4751 
  4752 static void
  4753 pgtk_buffer_flipping_unblocked_hook (struct frame *f)
  4754 {
  4755   block_input ();
  4756   flip_cr_context (f);
  4757   gtk_widget_queue_draw (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f));
  4758   unblock_input ();
  4759 }
