  4818 
  4819 struct pgtk_window_is_of_frame_recursive_t
  4820 {
  4821   GdkWindow *window;
  4822   bool result;
  4823   GtkWidget *emacs_gtk_fixed;   /* stop on emacsgtkfixed other than this. */
  4824 };
  4825 
  4826 static void
  4827 pgtk_window_is_of_frame_recursive (GtkWidget *widget, gpointer data)
  4828 {
  4829   struct pgtk_window_is_of_frame_recursive_t *datap = data;
  4830 
  4831   if (datap->result)
  4832     return;
  4833 
  4834   if (EMACS_IS_FIXED (widget) && widget != datap->emacs_gtk_fixed)
  4835     return;
  4836 
  4837   if (gtk_widget_get_window (widget) == datap->window)
  4838     {
  4839       datap->result = true;
  4840       return;
  4841     }
  4842 
  4843   if (GTK_IS_CONTAINER (widget))
  4844     gtk_container_foreach (GTK_CONTAINER (widget),
  4845                            pgtk_window_is_of_frame_recursive, datap);
  4846 }
  4847 
  4848 static bool
  4849 pgtk_window_is_of_frame (struct frame *f, GdkWindow *window)
  4850 {
  4851   struct pgtk_window_is_of_frame_recursive_t data;
  4852   data.window = window;
  4853   data.result = false;
  4854   data.emacs_gtk_fixed = FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f);
  4855   pgtk_window_is_of_frame_recursive (FRAME_WIDGET (f), &data);
  4856   return data.result;
  4857 }
  4858 
  4859 /* Like x_window_to_frame but also compares the window with the widget's
  4860    windows.  */
  4861 static struct frame *
  4862 pgtk_any_window_to_frame (GdkWindow *window)
  4863 {
  4864   Lisp_Object tail, frame;
  4865   struct frame *f, *found = NULL;
  4866 
  4867   if (window == NULL)
  4868     return NULL;
  4869 
  4870   FOR_EACH_FRAME (tail, frame)
  4871     {
  4872       if (found)
  4873         break;
  4874       f = XFRAME (frame);
  4875       if (FRAME_PGTK_P (f))
  4876         {
  4877           if (pgtk_window_is_of_frame (f, window))
  4878             found = f;
  4879         }
  4880     }
  4881 
  4882   return found;
  4883 }
  4884 
  4885 static gboolean
  4886 pgtk_handle_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event, gpointer *data)
  4887 {
  4888   struct frame *f;
  4889   union buffered_input_event inev;
  4890   GtkWidget *frame_widget;
  4891   gint x, y;
  4892 
  4893   if (event->type == GDK_TOUCHPAD_PINCH
  4894       && (event->touchpad_pinch.phase
  4895           != GDK_TOUCHPAD_GESTURE_PHASE_END))
  4896     {
  4897       f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  4898       frame_widget = FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f);
  4899 
  4900       gtk_widget_translate_coordinates (widget, frame_widget,
  4901                                         lrint (event->touchpad_pinch.x),
  4902                                         lrint (event->touchpad_pinch.y),
  4903                                         &x, &y);
  4904       if (f)
  4905         {
  4906 
  4907           inev.ie.kind = PINCH_EVENT;
  4908           XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  4909           XSETINT (inev.ie.x, x);
  4910           XSETINT (inev.ie.y, y);
  4911           inev.ie.arg = list4 (make_float (event->touchpad_pinch.dx),
  4912                                make_float (event->touchpad_pinch.dy),
  4913                                make_float (event->touchpad_pinch.scale),
  4914                                make_float (event->touchpad_pinch.angle_delta));
  4915           inev.ie.modifiers = pgtk_gtk_to_emacs_modifiers (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f),
  4916                                                            event->touchpad_pinch.state);
  4917           inev.ie.device
  4918             = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  4919           evq_enqueue (&inev);
  4920         }
  4921 
  4922       return TRUE;
  4923     }
  4924   return FALSE;
  4925 }
  4926 
  4927 static void
  4928 pgtk_fill_rectangle (struct frame *f, unsigned long color, int x, int y,
  4929                      int width, int height, bool respect_alpha_background)
  4930 {
  4931   cairo_t *cr;
  4932   cr = pgtk_begin_cr_clip (f);
  4933   pgtk_set_cr_source_with_color (f, color, respect_alpha_background);
  4934   cairo_rectangle (cr, x, y, width, height);
  4935   cairo_fill (cr);
  4936   pgtk_end_cr_clip (f);
  4937 }
  4938 
  4939 void
  4940 pgtk_clear_under_internal_border (struct frame *f)
  4941 {
  4942   if (FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f) > 0
  4943       && (!FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f)
  4944           || gtk_widget_get_realized (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f))))
  4945     {
  4946       int border = FRAME_INTERNAL_BORDER_WIDTH (f);
  4947       int width = FRAME_PIXEL_WIDTH (f);
  4948       int height = FRAME_PIXEL_HEIGHT (f);
  4949       int margin = FRAME_TOP_MARGIN_HEIGHT (f);
  4950       int face_id =
  4951         (FRAME_PARENT_FRAME (f)
  4952          ? (!NILP (Vface_remapping_alist)
  4953             ? lookup_basic_face (NULL, f, CHILD_FRAME_BORDER_FACE_ID)
  4954             : CHILD_FRAME_BORDER_FACE_ID)
  4955          : (!NILP (Vface_remapping_alist)
  4956             ? lookup_basic_face (NULL, f, INTERNAL_BORDER_FACE_ID)
  4957             : INTERNAL_BORDER_FACE_ID));
  4958       struct face *face = FACE_FROM_ID_OR_NULL (f, face_id);
  4959 
  4960       block_input ();
  4961 
  4962       if (face)
  4963         {
  4964 #define x_fill_rectangle(f, gc, x, y, w, h) \
  4965             fill_background_by_face (f, face, x, y, w, h)
  4966           x_fill_rectangle (f, gc, 0, margin, width, border);
  4967           x_fill_rectangle (f, gc, 0, 0, border, height);
  4968           x_fill_rectangle (f, gc, width - border, 0, border, height);
  4969           x_fill_rectangle (f, gc, 0, height - border, width, border);
  4970 #undef x_fill_rectangle
  4971         }
  4972       else
  4973         {
  4974 #define x_clear_area(f, x, y, w, h)  pgtk_clear_area (f, x, y, w, h)
  4975           x_clear_area (f, 0, 0, border, height);
  4976           x_clear_area (f, 0, margin, width, border);
  4977           x_clear_area (f, width - border, 0, border, height);
  4978           x_clear_area (f, 0, height - border, width, border);
  4979 #undef x_clear_area
  4980         }
  4981 
  4982       unblock_input ();
  4983     }
  4984 }
  4985 
  4986 static gboolean
  4987 pgtk_handle_draw (GtkWidget *widget, cairo_t *cr, gpointer *data)
  4988 {
  4989   struct frame *f;
  4990 
  4991   GdkWindow *win = gtk_widget_get_window (widget);
  4992 
  4993   if (win != NULL)
  4994     {
  4995       cairo_surface_t *src = NULL;
  4996       f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (win);
  4997       if (f != NULL)
  4998         {
  4999           src = FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->cr_surface_visible_bell;
  5000           if (src == NULL && FRAME_CR_ACTIVE_CONTEXT (f) != NULL)
  5001             src = cairo_get_target (FRAME_CR_ACTIVE_CONTEXT (f));
  5002         }
  5003       if (src != NULL)
  5004         {
  5005           cairo_set_source_surface (cr, src, 0, 0);
  5006           cairo_paint (cr);
  5007         }
  5008     }
  5009   return FALSE;
  5010 }
  5011 
  5012 static void
  5013 size_allocate (GtkWidget *widget, GtkAllocation *alloc,
  5014                gpointer user_data)
  5015 {
  5016   struct frame *f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5017 
  5018   if (!f)
  5019     f = user_data;
  5020 
  5021   if (f)
  5022     {
  5023       xg_frame_resized (f, alloc->width, alloc->height);
  5024       pgtk_cr_update_surface_desired_size (f, alloc->width, alloc->height, false);
  5025     }
  5026 }
  5027 
  5028 static void
  5029 get_modifier_values (int *mod_ctrl, int *mod_meta, int *mod_alt,
  5030                      int *mod_hyper, int *mod_super)
  5031 {
  5032   Lisp_Object tem;
  5033 
  5034   *mod_ctrl = ctrl_modifier;
  5035   *mod_meta = meta_modifier;
  5036   *mod_alt = alt_modifier;
  5037   *mod_hyper = hyper_modifier;
  5038   *mod_super = super_modifier;
  5039 
  5040   tem = Fget (Vx_ctrl_keysym, Qmodifier_value);
  5041   if (INTEGERP (tem))
  5042     *mod_ctrl = XFIXNUM (tem) & INT_MAX;
  5043   tem = Fget (Vx_alt_keysym, Qmodifier_value);
  5044   if (INTEGERP (tem))
  5045     *mod_alt = XFIXNUM (tem) & INT_MAX;
  5046   tem = Fget (Vx_meta_keysym, Qmodifier_value);
  5047   if (INTEGERP (tem))
  5048     *mod_meta = XFIXNUM (tem) & INT_MAX;
  5049   tem = Fget (Vx_hyper_keysym, Qmodifier_value);
  5050   if (INTEGERP (tem))
  5051     *mod_hyper = XFIXNUM (tem) & INT_MAX;
  5052   tem = Fget (Vx_super_keysym, Qmodifier_value);
  5053   if (INTEGERP (tem))
  5054     *mod_super = XFIXNUM (tem) & INT_MAX;
  5055 }
  5056 
  5057 int
  5058 pgtk_gtk_to_emacs_modifiers (struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo, int state)
  5059 {
  5060   int mod_ctrl;
  5061   int mod_meta;
  5062   int mod_alt;
  5063   int mod_hyper;
  5064   int mod_super;
  5065   int mod;
  5066 
  5067   get_modifier_values (&mod_ctrl, &mod_meta, &mod_alt, &mod_hyper,
  5068                        &mod_super);
  5069 
  5070   mod = 0;
  5071   if (state & GDK_SHIFT_MASK)
  5072     mod |= shift_modifier;
  5073   if (state & GDK_CONTROL_MASK)
  5074     mod |= mod_ctrl;
  5075   if (state & GDK_META_MASK || state & GDK_MOD1_MASK)
  5076     mod |= mod_meta;
  5077   if (state & GDK_SUPER_MASK)
  5078     mod |= mod_super;
  5079   if (state & GDK_HYPER_MASK)
  5080     mod |= mod_hyper;
  5081 
  5082   return mod;
  5083 }
  5084 
  5085 int
  5086 pgtk_emacs_to_gtk_modifiers (struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo, int state)
  5087 {
  5088   int mod_ctrl;
  5089   int mod_meta;
  5090   int mod_alt;
  5091   int mod_hyper;
  5092   int mod_super;
  5093   int mask;
  5094 
  5095   get_modifier_values (&mod_ctrl, &mod_meta, &mod_alt, &mod_hyper,
  5096                        &mod_super);
  5097 
  5098   mask = 0;
  5099   if (state & mod_super)
  5100     mask |= GDK_SUPER_MASK;
  5101   if (state & mod_hyper)
  5102     mask |= GDK_HYPER_MASK;
  5103   if (state & shift_modifier)
  5104     mask |= GDK_SHIFT_MASK;
  5105   if (state & mod_ctrl)
  5106     mask |= GDK_CONTROL_MASK;
  5107   if (state & mod_meta)
  5108     mask |= GDK_MOD1_MASK;
  5109   return mask;
  5110 }
  5111 
  5112 #define IsCursorKey(keysym)       (0xff50 <= (keysym) && (keysym) < 0xff60)
  5113 #define IsMiscFunctionKey(keysym) (0xff60 <= (keysym) && (keysym) < 0xff6c)
  5114 #define IsKeypadKey(keysym)       (0xff80 <= (keysym) && (keysym) < 0xffbe)
  5115 #define IsFunctionKey(keysym)     (0xffbe <= (keysym) && (keysym) < 0xffe1)
  5116 #define IsModifierKey(keysym)                                                   \
  5117   ((((keysym) >= GDK_KEY_Shift_L) && ((keysym) <= GDK_KEY_Hyper_R))             \
  5118    || (((keysym) >= GDK_KEY_ISO_Lock) && ((keysym) <= GDK_KEY_ISO_Level5_Lock)) \
  5119    || ((keysym) == GDK_KEY_Mode_switch)                                         \
  5120    || ((keysym) == GDK_KEY_Num_Lock))
  5121 
  5122 
  5123 void
  5124 pgtk_enqueue_string (struct frame *f, gchar *str)
  5125 {
  5126   gunichar *ustr, *uptr;
  5127 
  5128   uptr = ustr = g_utf8_to_ucs4 (str, -1, NULL, NULL, NULL);
  5129   if (ustr == NULL)
  5130     return;
  5131   for (; *ustr != 0; ustr++)
  5132     {
  5133       union buffered_input_event inev;
  5134       Lisp_Object c = make_fixnum (*ustr);
  5135       EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5136       inev.ie.kind = (SINGLE_BYTE_CHAR_P (XFIXNAT (c))
  5137                       ? ASCII_KEYSTROKE_EVENT
  5138                       : MULTIBYTE_CHAR_KEYSTROKE_EVENT);
  5139       inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5140       inev.ie.code = XFIXNAT (c);
  5141       XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  5142       inev.ie.modifiers = 0;
  5143       inev.ie.timestamp = 0;
  5144       evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5145     }
  5146 
  5147   g_free (uptr);
  5148 }
  5149 
  5150 void
  5151 pgtk_enqueue_preedit (struct frame *f, Lisp_Object preedit)
  5152 {
  5153   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5154   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5155   inev.ie.kind = PREEDIT_TEXT_EVENT;
  5156   inev.ie.arg = preedit;
  5157   inev.ie.code = 0;
  5158   XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  5159   inev.ie.modifiers = 0;
  5160   inev.ie.timestamp = 0;
  5161   evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5162 }
  5163 
  5164 static gboolean
  5165 key_press_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event, gpointer *user_data)
  5166 {
  5167   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5168   ptrdiff_t nbytes;
  5169   Mouse_HLInfo *hlinfo;
  5170   struct frame *f;
  5171   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  5172 
  5173   f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5174   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5175   hlinfo = MOUSE_HL_INFO (f);
  5176   nbytes = 0;
  5177 
  5178   /* If mouse-highlight is an integer, input clears out
  5179      mouse highlighting.  */
  5180   if (!hlinfo->mouse_face_hidden && INTEGERP (Vmouse_highlight))
  5181     {
  5182       clear_mouse_face (hlinfo);
  5183       hlinfo->mouse_face_hidden = true;
  5184     }
  5185 
  5186   if (f != 0)
  5187     {
  5188       guint keysym, orig_keysym;
  5189       /* al%imercury@uunet.uu.net says that making this 81
  5190          instead of 80 fixed a bug whereby meta chars made
  5191          his Emacs hang.
  5192 
  5193          It seems that some version of XmbLookupString has
  5194          a bug of not returning XBufferOverflow in
  5195          status_return even if the input is too long to
  5196          fit in 81 bytes.  So, we must prepare sufficient
  5197          bytes for copy_buffer.  513 bytes (256 chars for
  5198          two-byte character set) seems to be a fairly good
  5199          approximation.  -- 2000.8.10 handa@etl.go.jp  */
  5200       unsigned char copy_buffer[513];
  5201       unsigned char *copy_bufptr = copy_buffer;
  5202       int copy_bufsiz = sizeof (copy_buffer);
  5203       int modifiers;
  5204       Lisp_Object c;
  5205       guint state;
  5206 
  5207       dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f);
  5208 
  5209       /* Set the last user time for pgtk_focus_frame to work
  5210          correctly.  */
  5211       dpyinfo->last_user_time = event->key.time;
  5212 
  5213       state = event->key.state;
  5214 
  5215       /* While super is pressed, the input method will always always
  5216          resend the key events ignoring super.  As a workaround, don't
  5217          filter key events with super or hyper pressed.  */
  5218       if (!(event->key.state & (GDK_SUPER_MASK | GDK_HYPER_MASK)))
  5219         {
  5220           if (pgtk_im_filter_keypress (f, &event->key))
  5221             return TRUE;
  5222         }
  5223 
  5224       state |= pgtk_emacs_to_gtk_modifiers (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f),
  5225                                             extra_keyboard_modifiers);
  5226       modifiers = state;
  5227 
  5228       /* This will have to go some day...  */
  5229 
  5230       /* make_lispy_event turns chars into control chars.
  5231          Don't do it here because XLookupString is too eager.  */
  5232       state &= ~GDK_CONTROL_MASK;
  5233       state &= ~(GDK_META_MASK
  5234                  | GDK_SUPER_MASK | GDK_HYPER_MASK | GDK_MOD1_MASK);
  5235 
  5236       nbytes = event->key.length;
  5237       if (nbytes > copy_bufsiz)
  5238         nbytes = copy_bufsiz;
  5239       memcpy (copy_bufptr, event->key.string, nbytes);
  5240 
  5241       keysym = event->key.keyval;
  5242       orig_keysym = keysym;
  5243 
  5244       /* Common for all keysym input events.  */
  5245       XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  5246       inev.ie.modifiers
  5247         = pgtk_gtk_to_emacs_modifiers (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), modifiers);
  5248       inev.ie.timestamp = event->key.time;
  5249 
  5250       /* First deal with keysyms which have defined
  5251          translations to characters.  */
  5252       if (keysym >= 32 && keysym < 128)
  5253         /* Avoid explicitly decoding each ASCII character.  */
  5254         {
  5255           inev.ie.kind = ASCII_KEYSTROKE_EVENT;
  5256           inev.ie.code = keysym;
  5257 
  5258           inev.ie.device
  5259             = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  5260           goto done;
  5261         }
  5262 
  5263       /* Keysyms directly mapped to Unicode characters.  */
  5264       if (keysym >= 0x01000000 && keysym <= 0x0110FFFF)
  5265         {
  5266           if (keysym < 0x01000080)
  5267             inev.ie.kind = ASCII_KEYSTROKE_EVENT;
  5268           else
  5269             inev.ie.kind = MULTIBYTE_CHAR_KEYSTROKE_EVENT;
  5270           inev.ie.code = keysym & 0xFFFFFF;
  5271 
  5272           inev.ie.device
  5273             = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  5274           goto done;
  5275         }
  5276 
  5277       /* Now non-ASCII.  */
  5278       if (HASH_TABLE_P (Vpgtk_keysym_table)
  5279           && (c = Fgethash (make_fixnum (keysym),
  5280                             Vpgtk_keysym_table, Qnil), FIXNATP (c)))
  5281         {
  5282           inev.ie.kind = (SINGLE_BYTE_CHAR_P (XFIXNAT (c))
  5283                           ? ASCII_KEYSTROKE_EVENT
  5284                           : MULTIBYTE_CHAR_KEYSTROKE_EVENT);
  5285           inev.ie.code = XFIXNAT (c);
  5286 
  5287           inev.ie.device
  5288             = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  5289           goto done;
  5290         }
  5291 
  5292       /* Random non-modifier sorts of keysyms.  */
  5293       if (((keysym >= GDK_KEY_BackSpace && keysym <= GDK_KEY_Escape)
  5294            || keysym == GDK_KEY_Delete
  5295 #ifdef GDK_KEY_ISO_Left_Tab
  5296            || (keysym >= GDK_KEY_ISO_Left_Tab && keysym <= GDK_KEY_ISO_Enter)
  5297 #endif
  5298            || IsCursorKey (keysym)      /* 0xff50 <= x < 0xff60 */
  5299            || IsMiscFunctionKey (keysym)        /* 0xff60 <= x < VARIES */
  5300 #ifdef HPUX
  5301            /* This recognizes the "extended function
  5302               keys".  It seems there's no cleaner way.
  5303               Test IsModifierKey to avoid handling
  5304               mode_switch incorrectly.  */
  5305            || (GDK_KEY_Select <= keysym && keysym < GDK_KEY_KP_Space)
  5306 #endif
  5307 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_circumflex
  5308            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_circumflex
  5309 #endif
  5310 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_grave
  5311            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_grave
  5312 #endif
  5313 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_tilde
  5314            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_tilde
  5315 #endif
  5316 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_diaeresis
  5317            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_diaeresis
  5318 #endif
  5319 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_macron
  5320            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_macron
  5321 #endif
  5322 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_degree
  5323            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_degree
  5324 #endif
  5325 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_acute
  5326            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_acute
  5327 #endif
  5328 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_cedilla
  5329            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_cedilla
  5330 #endif
  5331 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_breve
  5332            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_breve
  5333 #endif
  5334 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_ogonek
  5335            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_ogonek
  5336 #endif
  5337 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_caron
  5338            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_caron
  5339 #endif
  5340 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_doubleacute
  5341            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_doubleacute
  5342 #endif
  5343 #ifdef GDK_KEY_dead_abovedot
  5344            || orig_keysym == GDK_KEY_dead_abovedot
  5345 #endif
  5346            || IsKeypadKey (keysym)      /* 0xff80 <= x < 0xffbe */
  5347            || IsFunctionKey (keysym)    /* 0xffbe <= x < 0xffe1 */
  5348            /* Any "vendor-specific" key is ok.  */
  5349            || (orig_keysym & (1 << 28))
  5350            || (keysym != GDK_KEY_VoidSymbol && nbytes == 0))
  5351           && !(event->key.is_modifier
  5352                || IsModifierKey (orig_keysym)
  5353                /* The symbols from GDK_KEY_ISO_Lock
  5354                   to GDK_KEY_ISO_Last_Group_Lock
  5355                   don't have real modifiers but
  5356                   should be treated similarly to
  5357                   Mode_switch by Emacs. */
  5358 #if defined GDK_KEY_ISO_Lock && defined GDK_KEY_ISO_Last_Group_Lock
  5359                || (GDK_KEY_ISO_Lock <= orig_keysym
  5360                    && orig_keysym <= GDK_KEY_ISO_Last_Group_Lock)
  5361 #endif
  5362           ))
  5363         {
  5364           /* make_lispy_event will convert this to a symbolic
  5365              key.  */
  5366           inev.ie.kind = NON_ASCII_KEYSTROKE_EVENT;
  5367           inev.ie.code = keysym;
  5368 
  5369           inev.ie.device
  5370             = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  5371           goto done;
  5372         }
  5373 
  5374       {
  5375         inev.ie.kind = MULTIBYTE_CHAR_KEYSTROKE_EVENT;
  5376         inev.ie.arg = make_unibyte_string ((char *) copy_bufptr, nbytes);
  5377         inev.ie.device
  5378           = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  5379 
  5380         if (keysym == GDK_KEY_VoidSymbol)
  5381           goto done;
  5382       }
  5383     }
  5384 
  5385 done:
  5386   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5387     {
  5388       XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  5389       evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5390     }
  5391 
  5392   return TRUE;
  5393 }
  5394 
  5395 static struct pgtk_display_info *
  5396 pgtk_display_info_for_display (GdkDisplay *dpy)
  5397 {
  5398   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  5399 
  5400   for (dpyinfo = x_display_list; dpyinfo; dpyinfo = dpyinfo->next)
  5401     {
  5402       if (dpyinfo->display == dpy)
  5403         return dpyinfo;
  5404     }
  5405 
  5406   return NULL;
  5407 }
  5408 
  5409 static gboolean
  5410 key_release_event (GtkWidget *widget,
  5411                    GdkEvent *event,
  5412                    gpointer *user_data)
  5413 {
  5414   GdkDisplay *display;
  5415   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  5416 
  5417   display = gtk_widget_get_display (widget);
  5418   dpyinfo = pgtk_display_info_for_display (display);
  5419 
  5420   if (dpyinfo)
  5421     /* This is needed on Wayland because of some brain dead
  5422        compositors.  Without them, we would not have to keep track of
  5423        the serial of key release events.  */
  5424     dpyinfo->last_user_time = event->key.time;
  5425 
  5426   return TRUE;
  5427 }
  5428 
  5429 static gboolean
  5430 configure_event (GtkWidget *widget,
  5431                  GdkEvent *event,
  5432                  gpointer *user_data)
  5433 {
  5434   struct frame *f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (event->configure.window);
  5435 
  5436   if (f && widget == FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f))
  5437     {
  5438       if (any_help_event_p)
  5439         {
  5440           Lisp_Object frame;
  5441           if (f)
  5442             XSETFRAME (frame, f);
  5443           else
  5444             frame = Qnil;
  5445           help_echo_string = Qnil;
  5446           gen_help_event (Qnil, frame, Qnil, Qnil, 0);
  5447         }
  5448 
  5449       if (f->win_gravity == NorthWestGravity)
  5450         gtk_window_get_position (GTK_WINDOW (widget),
  5451                                  &f->left_pos, &f->top_pos);
  5452       else
  5453         {
  5454           f->top_pos = event->configure.y;
  5455           f->left_pos = event->configure.x;
  5456         }
  5457     }
  5458   return FALSE;
  5459 }
  5460 
  5461 static gboolean
  5462 map_event (GtkWidget *widget,
  5463            GdkEvent *event,
  5464            gpointer *user_data)
  5465 {
  5466   struct frame *f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (event->any.window);
  5467   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5468 
  5469   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5470   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5471   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5472 
  5473   if (f)
  5474     {
  5475       bool iconified = FRAME_ICONIFIED_P (f);
  5476 
  5477       /* Check if fullscreen was specified before we where mapped the
  5478          first time, i.e. from the command line.  */
  5479       if (!FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->has_been_visible)
  5480         set_fullscreen_state (f);
  5481 
  5482       if (!iconified)
  5483         {
  5484           /* The `z-group' is reset every time a frame becomes
  5485              invisible.  Handle this here.  */
  5486           if (FRAME_Z_GROUP (f) == z_group_above)
  5487             pgtk_set_z_group (f, Qabove, Qnil);
  5488           else if (FRAME_Z_GROUP (f) == z_group_below)
  5489             pgtk_set_z_group (f, Qbelow, Qnil);
  5490         }
  5491 
  5492       SET_FRAME_VISIBLE (f, 1);
  5493       SET_FRAME_ICONIFIED (f, false);
  5494       FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->has_been_visible = true;
  5495 
  5496       if (iconified)
  5497         {
  5498           inev.ie.kind = DEICONIFY_EVENT;
  5499           XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  5500         }
  5501     }
  5502 
  5503   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5504     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5505   return FALSE;
  5506 }
  5507 
  5508 static gboolean
  5509 window_state_event (GtkWidget *widget,
  5510                     GdkEvent *event,
  5511                     gpointer *user_data)
  5512 {
  5513   struct frame *f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (event->window_state.window);
  5514   GdkWindowState new_state;
  5515   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5516 
  5517   new_state = event->window_state.new_window_state;
  5518 
  5519   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5520   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5521   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5522 
  5523   if (new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_FULLSCREEN)
  5524     store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qfullboth);
  5525   else if (new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_MAXIMIZED)
  5526     store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qmaximized);
  5527   else if ((new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_TOP_TILED)
  5528            && (new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_BOTTOM_TILED)
  5529            && !(new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_TOP_RESIZABLE)
  5530            && !(new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_BOTTOM_RESIZABLE))
  5531     store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qfullheight);
  5532   else if ((new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_LEFT_TILED)
  5533            && (new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_RIGHT_TILED)
  5534            && !(new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_LEFT_RESIZABLE)
  5535            && !(new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_RIGHT_RESIZABLE))
  5536     store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qfullwidth);
  5537   else
  5538     store_frame_param (f, Qfullscreen, Qnil);
  5539 
  5540   /* The Wayland protocol provides no way for the client to know
  5541      whether or not one of its toplevels has actually been
  5542      deiconified.  It only provides a request for clients to iconify a
  5543      toplevel, without even the ability to determine whether or not
  5544      the iconification request was rejected by the display server.
  5545 
  5546      GDK computes the iconified state by sending a window state event
  5547      containing only GDK_WINDOW_STATE_ICONIFIED immediately after
  5548      gtk_window_iconify is called.  That is error-prone if the request
  5549      to iconify the frame was rejected by the display server, but is
  5550      not the main problem here, as Wayland compositors only rarely
  5551      reject such requests.  GDK also assumes that it can clear the
  5552      iconified state upon receiving the next toplevel configure event
  5553      from the display server.  Unfortunately, such events can be sent
  5554      by Wayland compositors while the frame is iconified, and may also
  5555      not be sent upon deiconification.  So, no matter what Emacs does,
  5556      the iconification state of a frame is likely to be wrong under
  5557      one situation or another.  */
  5558 
  5559   if (new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_ICONIFIED)
  5560     {
  5561       SET_FRAME_ICONIFIED (f, true);
  5562       SET_FRAME_VISIBLE (f, false);
  5563     }
  5564   else
  5565     {
  5566       FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->has_been_visible = true;
  5567       inev.ie.kind = DEICONIFY_EVENT;
  5568       XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  5569       SET_FRAME_ICONIFIED (f, false);
  5570       SET_FRAME_VISIBLE (f, true);
  5571     }
  5572 
  5573   if (new_state & GDK_WINDOW_STATE_STICKY)
  5574     store_frame_param (f, Qsticky, Qt);
  5575   else
  5576     store_frame_param (f, Qsticky, Qnil);
  5577 
  5578   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5579     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5580   return FALSE;
  5581 }
  5582 
  5583 static gboolean
  5584 delete_event (GtkWidget *widget,
  5585               GdkEvent *event, gpointer *user_data)
  5586 {
  5587   struct frame *f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (event->any.window);
  5588   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5589 
  5590   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5591   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5592   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5593 
  5594   if (f)
  5595     {
  5596       inev.ie.kind = DELETE_WINDOW_EVENT;
  5597       XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  5598     }
  5599 
  5600   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5601     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5602   return TRUE;
  5603 }
  5604 
  5605 /* The focus may have changed.  Figure out if it is a real focus change,
  5606    by checking both FocusIn/Out and Enter/LeaveNotify events.
  5607 
  5608    Returns FOCUS_IN_EVENT event in *BUFP. */
  5609 
  5610 /* Handle FocusIn and FocusOut state changes for FRAME.
  5611    If FRAME has focus and there exists more than one frame, puts
  5612    a FOCUS_IN_EVENT into *BUFP.  */
  5613 
  5614 static void
  5615 pgtk_focus_changed (gboolean is_enter, int state,
  5616                     struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo, struct frame *frame,
  5617                     union buffered_input_event *bufp)
  5618 {
  5619   if (is_enter)
  5620     {
  5621       if (dpyinfo->x_focus_event_frame != frame)
  5622         {
  5623           pgtk_new_focus_frame (dpyinfo, frame);
  5624           dpyinfo->x_focus_event_frame = frame;
  5625 
  5626           /* Don't stop displaying the initial startup message
  5627              for a switch-frame event we don't need.  */
  5628           /* When run as a daemon, Vterminal_frame is always NIL.  */
  5629           bufp->ie.arg = (((NILP (Vterminal_frame)
  5630                             || !FRAME_PGTK_P (XFRAME (Vterminal_frame))
  5631                             || EQ (Fdaemonp (), Qt))
  5632                            && CONSP (Vframe_list)
  5633                            && !NILP (XCDR (Vframe_list))) ? Qt : Qnil);
  5634           bufp->ie.kind = FOCUS_IN_EVENT;
  5635           XSETFRAME (bufp->ie.frame_or_window, frame);
  5636         }
  5637 
  5638       frame->output_data.pgtk->focus_state |= state;
  5639 
  5640     }
  5641   else
  5642     {
  5643       frame->output_data.pgtk->focus_state &= ~state;
  5644 
  5645       if (dpyinfo->x_focus_event_frame == frame)
  5646         {
  5647           dpyinfo->x_focus_event_frame = 0;
  5648           pgtk_new_focus_frame (dpyinfo, NULL);
  5649 
  5650           bufp->ie.kind = FOCUS_OUT_EVENT;
  5651           XSETFRAME (bufp->ie.frame_or_window, frame);
  5652         }
  5653 
  5654       if (frame->pointer_invisible)
  5655         pgtk_toggle_invisible_pointer (frame, false);
  5656     }
  5657 }
  5658 
  5659 static gboolean
  5660 enter_notify_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event,
  5661                     gpointer *user_data)
  5662 {
  5663   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5664   struct frame *frame
  5665     = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5666 
  5667   if (frame == NULL)
  5668     return FALSE;
  5669 
  5670   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame);
  5671   struct frame *focus_frame = dpyinfo->x_focus_frame;
  5672   int focus_state
  5673     = focus_frame ? focus_frame->output_data.pgtk->focus_state : 0;
  5674 
  5675   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5676   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5677   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5678 
  5679   if (event->crossing.detail != GDK_NOTIFY_INFERIOR
  5680       && event->crossing.focus && !(focus_state & FOCUS_EXPLICIT))
  5681     pgtk_focus_changed (TRUE, FOCUS_IMPLICIT, dpyinfo, frame, &inev);
  5682   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5683     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5684   return TRUE;
  5685 }
  5686 
  5687 static gboolean
  5688 leave_notify_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event,
  5689                     gpointer *user_data)
  5690 {
  5691   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5692   struct frame *frame
  5693     = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5694 
  5695   if (frame == NULL)
  5696     return FALSE;
  5697 
  5698   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame);
  5699   struct frame *focus_frame = dpyinfo->x_focus_frame;
  5700   int focus_state
  5701     = focus_frame ? focus_frame->output_data.pgtk->focus_state : 0;
  5702   Mouse_HLInfo *hlinfo = MOUSE_HL_INFO (frame);
  5703 
  5704   if (frame == hlinfo->mouse_face_mouse_frame)
  5705     {
  5706       /* If we move outside the frame, then we're
  5707          certainly no longer on any text in the frame.  */
  5708       clear_mouse_face (hlinfo);
  5709       hlinfo->mouse_face_mouse_frame = 0;
  5710     }
  5711 
  5712   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5713   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5714   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5715 
  5716   if (event->crossing.detail != GDK_NOTIFY_INFERIOR
  5717       && event->crossing.focus && !(focus_state & FOCUS_EXPLICIT))
  5718     pgtk_focus_changed (FALSE, FOCUS_IMPLICIT, dpyinfo, frame, &inev);
  5719 
  5720   if (frame)
  5721     {
  5722       if (any_help_event_p)
  5723         {
  5724           Lisp_Object frame_obj;
  5725           XSETFRAME (frame_obj, frame);
  5726           help_echo_string = Qnil;
  5727           gen_help_event (Qnil, frame_obj, Qnil, Qnil, 0);
  5728         }
  5729     }
  5730 
  5731   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5732     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5733   return TRUE;
  5734 }
  5735 
  5736 static gboolean
  5737 focus_in_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event, gpointer *user_data)
  5738 {
  5739   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5740   struct frame *frame
  5741     = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5742 
  5743   if (frame == NULL)
  5744     return TRUE;
  5745 
  5746   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5747   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5748   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5749 
  5750   pgtk_focus_changed (TRUE, FOCUS_EXPLICIT,
  5751                       FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame), frame, &inev);
  5752   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5753     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5754 
  5755   pgtk_im_focus_in (frame);
  5756 
  5757   return TRUE;
  5758 }
  5759 
  5760 static gboolean
  5761 focus_out_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event, gpointer *user_data)
  5762 {
  5763   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5764   struct frame *frame
  5765     = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5766 
  5767   if (frame == NULL)
  5768     return TRUE;
  5769 
  5770   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5771   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5772   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5773 
  5774   pgtk_focus_changed (FALSE, FOCUS_EXPLICIT,
  5775                       FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame), frame, &inev);
  5776   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5777     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5778 
  5779   pgtk_im_focus_out (frame);
  5780 
  5781   return TRUE;
  5782 }
  5783 
  5784 /* Function to report a mouse movement to the mainstream Emacs code.
  5785    The input handler calls this.
  5786 
  5787    We have received a mouse movement event, which is given in *event.
  5788    If the mouse is over a different glyph than it was last time, tell
  5789    the mainstream emacs code by setting mouse_moved.  If not, ask for
  5790    another motion event, so we can check again the next time it moves.  */
  5791 
  5792 static bool
  5793 note_mouse_movement (struct frame *frame,
  5794                      const GdkEventMotion *event)
  5795 {
  5796   XRectangle *r;
  5797   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  5798 
  5799   if (!FRAME_X_OUTPUT (frame))
  5800     return false;
  5801 
  5802   dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame);
  5803   dpyinfo->last_mouse_movement_time = event->time;
  5804   dpyinfo->last_mouse_motion_frame = frame;
  5805   dpyinfo->last_mouse_motion_x = event->x;
  5806   dpyinfo->last_mouse_motion_y = event->y;
  5807 
  5808   if (event->window != gtk_widget_get_window (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (frame)))
  5809     {
  5810       frame->mouse_moved = true;
  5811       dpyinfo->last_mouse_scroll_bar = NULL;
  5812       note_mouse_highlight (frame, -1, -1);
  5813       dpyinfo->last_mouse_glyph_frame = NULL;
  5814       frame->last_mouse_device
  5815         = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame),
  5816                                      (GdkEvent *) event);
  5817       return true;
  5818     }
  5819 
  5820 
  5821   /* Has the mouse moved off the glyph it was on at the last sighting?  */
  5822   r = &dpyinfo->last_mouse_glyph;
  5823   if (frame != dpyinfo->last_mouse_glyph_frame
  5824       || event->x < r->x || event->x >= r->x + r->width
  5825       || event->y < r->y || event->y >= r->y + r->height)
  5826     {
  5827       frame->mouse_moved = true;
  5828       dpyinfo->last_mouse_scroll_bar = NULL;
  5829       note_mouse_highlight (frame, event->x, event->y);
  5830       /* Remember which glyph we're now on.  */
  5831       remember_mouse_glyph (frame, event->x, event->y, r);
  5832       dpyinfo->last_mouse_glyph_frame = frame;
  5833       frame->last_mouse_device
  5834         = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame),
  5835                                      (GdkEvent *) event);
  5836       return true;
  5837     }
  5838 
  5839   return false;
  5840 }
  5841 
  5842 static gboolean
  5843 motion_notify_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event,
  5844                      gpointer *user_data)
  5845 {
  5846   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5847   struct frame *f, *frame;
  5848   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  5849   Mouse_HLInfo *hlinfo;
  5850 
  5851   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5852   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5853   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5854 
  5855   previous_help_echo_string = help_echo_string;
  5856   help_echo_string = Qnil;
  5857 
  5858   frame = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5859   dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame);
  5860   f = (gui_mouse_grabbed (dpyinfo) ? dpyinfo->last_mouse_frame
  5861        : pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget)));
  5862   hlinfo = MOUSE_HL_INFO (f);
  5863 
  5864   if (hlinfo->mouse_face_hidden)
  5865     {
  5866       hlinfo->mouse_face_hidden = false;
  5867       clear_mouse_face (hlinfo);
  5868     }
  5869 
  5870   if (f && xg_event_is_for_scrollbar (f, event, false))
  5871     f = 0;
  5872 
  5873   if (f)
  5874     {
  5875       /* Maybe generate a SELECT_WINDOW_EVENT for
  5876          `mouse-autoselect-window' but don't let popup menus
  5877          interfere with this (Bug#1261).  */
  5878       if (!NILP (Vmouse_autoselect_window)
  5879           /* Don't switch if we're currently in the minibuffer.
  5880              This tries to work around problems where the
  5881              minibuffer gets unselected unexpectedly, and where
  5882              you then have to move your mouse all the way down to
  5883              the minibuffer to select it.  */
  5884           && !MINI_WINDOW_P (XWINDOW (selected_window))
  5885           /* With `focus-follows-mouse' non-nil create an event
  5886              also when the target window is on another frame.  */
  5887           && (f == XFRAME (selected_frame) || !NILP (focus_follows_mouse)))
  5888         {
  5889           static Lisp_Object last_mouse_window;
  5890           Lisp_Object window = window_from_coordinates
  5891             (f, event->motion.x, event->motion.y, 0, false, false);
  5892 
  5893           /* A window will be autoselected only when it is not
  5894              selected now and the last mouse movement event was
  5895              not in it.  The remainder of the code is a bit vague
  5896              wrt what a "window" is.  For immediate autoselection,
  5897              the window is usually the entire window but for GTK
  5898              where the scroll bars don't count.  For delayed
  5899              autoselection the window is usually the window's text
  5900              area including the margins.  */
  5901           if (WINDOWP (window)
  5902               && !EQ (window, last_mouse_window)
  5903               && !EQ (window, selected_window))
  5904             {
  5905               inev.ie.kind = SELECT_WINDOW_EVENT;
  5906               inev.ie.frame_or_window = window;
  5907             }
  5908 
  5909           /* Remember the last window where we saw the mouse.  */
  5910           last_mouse_window = window;
  5911         }
  5912 
  5913       if (!note_mouse_movement (f, &event->motion))
  5914         help_echo_string = previous_help_echo_string;
  5915     }
  5916   else
  5917     /* If we move outside the frame, then we're
  5918        certainly no longer on any text in the frame.  */
  5919     clear_mouse_face (hlinfo);
  5920 
  5921   /* If the contents of the global variable help_echo_string
  5922      has changed, generate a HELP_EVENT.  */
  5923   int do_help = 0;
  5924   if (!NILP (help_echo_string) || !NILP (previous_help_echo_string))
  5925     do_help = 1;
  5926 
  5927   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  5928     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  5929 
  5930   if (do_help > 0)
  5931     {
  5932       Lisp_Object frame;
  5933 
  5934       if (f)
  5935         XSETFRAME (frame, f);
  5936       else
  5937         frame = Qnil;
  5938 
  5939       any_help_event_p = true;
  5940       gen_help_event (help_echo_string, frame, help_echo_window,
  5941                       help_echo_object, help_echo_pos);
  5942     }
  5943 
  5944   return TRUE;
  5945 }
  5946 
  5947 /* Prepare a mouse-event in *RESULT for placement in the input queue.
  5948 
  5949    If the event is a button press, then note that we have grabbed
  5950    the mouse.  */
  5951 
  5952 static Lisp_Object
  5953 construct_mouse_click (struct input_event *result,
  5954                        const GdkEventButton *event,
  5955                        struct frame *f)
  5956 {
  5957   /* Make the event type NO_EVENT; we'll change that when we decide
  5958      otherwise.  */
  5959   result->kind = MOUSE_CLICK_EVENT;
  5960   result->code = event->button - 1;
  5961   result->timestamp = event->time;
  5962   result->modifiers = (pgtk_gtk_to_emacs_modifiers (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f),
  5963                                                     event->state)
  5964                        | (event->type == GDK_BUTTON_RELEASE
  5965                           ? up_modifier : down_modifier));
  5966 
  5967   XSETINT (result->x, event->x);
  5968   XSETINT (result->y, event->y);
  5969   XSETFRAME (result->frame_or_window, f);
  5970   result->arg = Qnil;
  5971   result->device = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f),
  5972                                               (GdkEvent *) event);
  5973   return Qnil;
  5974 }
  5975 
  5976 static gboolean
  5977 button_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event,
  5978               gpointer *user_data)
  5979 {
  5980   union buffered_input_event inev;
  5981   struct frame *f, *frame;
  5982   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  5983 
  5984   /* If we decide we want to generate an event to be seen
  5985      by the rest of Emacs, we put it here.  */
  5986   bool tab_bar_p = false;
  5987   bool tool_bar_p = false;
  5988   Lisp_Object tab_bar_arg = Qnil;
  5989 
  5990   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  5991   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  5992   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  5993 
  5994   /* ignore double click and triple click. */
  5995   if (event->type != GDK_BUTTON_PRESS && event->type != GDK_BUTTON_RELEASE)
  5996     return TRUE;
  5997 
  5998   frame = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  5999   dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame);
  6000 
  6001   dpyinfo->last_mouse_glyph_frame = NULL;
  6002 
  6003   if (gui_mouse_grabbed (dpyinfo))
  6004     f = dpyinfo->last_mouse_frame;
  6005   else
  6006     {
  6007       f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  6008 
  6009       if (f && event->button.type == GDK_BUTTON_PRESS
  6010           && !FRAME_NO_ACCEPT_FOCUS (f))
  6011         {
  6012           /* When clicking into a child frame or when clicking
  6013              into a parent frame with the child frame selected and
  6014              `no-accept-focus' is not set, select the clicked
  6015              frame.  */
  6016           struct frame *hf = dpyinfo->highlight_frame;
  6017 
  6018           if (FRAME_PARENT_FRAME (f) || (hf && frame_ancestor_p (f, hf)))
  6019             {
  6020               block_input ();
  6021               gtk_widget_grab_focus (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f));
  6022 
  6023               if (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f))
  6024                 gtk_window_present (GTK_WINDOW (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f)));
  6025               unblock_input ();
  6026             }
  6027         }
  6028     }
  6029 
  6030   /* Set the last user time, used to activate the frame in
  6031      pgtk_focus_frame.  */
  6032   dpyinfo->last_user_time = event->button.time;
  6033 
  6034   if (f)
  6035     {
  6036       /* Is this in the tab-bar?  */
  6037       if (WINDOWP (f->tab_bar_window)
  6038           && WINDOW_TOTAL_LINES (XWINDOW (f->tab_bar_window)))
  6039         {
  6040           Lisp_Object window;
  6041           int x = event->button.x;
  6042           int y = event->button.y;
  6043 
  6044           window = window_from_coordinates (f, x, y, 0, true, true);
  6045           tab_bar_p = EQ (window, f->tab_bar_window);
  6046 
  6047           if (tab_bar_p)
  6048             tab_bar_arg = handle_tab_bar_click
  6049               (f, x, y, event->type == GDK_BUTTON_PRESS,
  6050                pgtk_gtk_to_emacs_modifiers (dpyinfo, event->button.state));
  6051         }
  6052 
  6053       if (!(tab_bar_p && NILP (tab_bar_arg)) && !tool_bar_p)
  6054         {
  6055           if (ignore_next_mouse_click_timeout)
  6056             {
  6057               if (event->type == GDK_BUTTON_PRESS
  6058                   && event->button.time > ignore_next_mouse_click_timeout)
  6059                 {
  6060                   ignore_next_mouse_click_timeout = 0;
  6061                   construct_mouse_click (&inev.ie, &event->button, f);
  6062                 }
  6063               if (event->type == GDK_BUTTON_RELEASE)
  6064                 ignore_next_mouse_click_timeout = 0;
  6065             }
  6066           else
  6067             construct_mouse_click (&inev.ie, &event->button, f);
  6068 
  6069           if (!NILP (tab_bar_arg))
  6070             inev.ie.arg = tab_bar_arg;
  6071         }
  6072     }
  6073 
  6074   if (event->type == GDK_BUTTON_PRESS)
  6075     {
  6076       dpyinfo->grabbed |= (1 << event->button.button);
  6077       dpyinfo->last_mouse_frame = f;
  6078 
  6079       if (dpyinfo->last_click_event != NULL)
  6080         gdk_event_free (dpyinfo->last_click_event);
  6081       dpyinfo->last_click_event = gdk_event_copy (event);
  6082     }
  6083   else
  6084     dpyinfo->grabbed &= ~(1 << event->button.button);
  6085 
  6086   /* Ignore any mouse motion that happened before this event;
  6087      any subsequent mouse-movement Emacs events should reflect
  6088      only motion after the ButtonPress/Release.  */
  6089   if (f != 0)
  6090     f->mouse_moved = false;
  6091 
  6092   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  6093     evq_enqueue (&inev);
  6094   return TRUE;
  6095 }
  6096 
  6097 static gboolean
  6098 scroll_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event, gpointer *user_data)
  6099 {
  6100   union buffered_input_event inev;
  6101   struct frame *f, *frame;
  6102   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  6103   GdkScrollDirection dir;
  6104   double delta_x, delta_y;
  6105 
  6106   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  6107   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  6108   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  6109 
  6110   frame = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  6111   dpyinfo = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (frame);
  6112 
  6113   if (gui_mouse_grabbed (dpyinfo))
  6114     f = dpyinfo->last_mouse_frame;
  6115   else
  6116     f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  6117 
  6118   inev.ie.kind = NO_EVENT;
  6119   inev.ie.timestamp = event->scroll.time;
  6120   inev.ie.modifiers
  6121     = pgtk_gtk_to_emacs_modifiers (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event->scroll.state);
  6122   XSETINT (inev.ie.x, event->scroll.x);
  6123   XSETINT (inev.ie.y, event->scroll.y);
  6124   XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  6125   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  6126 
  6127   if (gdk_event_is_scroll_stop_event (event))
  6128     {
  6129       inev.ie.kind = TOUCH_END_EVENT;
  6130       inev.ie.device
  6131         = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  6132       evq_enqueue (&inev);
  6133       return TRUE;
  6134     }
  6135 
  6136   if (gdk_event_get_scroll_direction (event, &dir))
  6137     {
  6138       switch (dir)
  6139         {
  6140         case GDK_SCROLL_UP:
  6141           inev.ie.kind = WHEEL_EVENT;
  6142           inev.ie.modifiers |= up_modifier;
  6143           break;
  6144         case GDK_SCROLL_DOWN:
  6145           inev.ie.kind = WHEEL_EVENT;
  6146           inev.ie.modifiers |= down_modifier;
  6147           break;
  6148         case GDK_SCROLL_LEFT:
  6149           inev.ie.kind = HORIZ_WHEEL_EVENT;
  6150           inev.ie.modifiers |= up_modifier;
  6151           break;
  6152         case GDK_SCROLL_RIGHT:
  6153           inev.ie.kind = HORIZ_WHEEL_EVENT;
  6154           inev.ie.modifiers |= down_modifier;
  6155           break;
  6156         case GDK_SCROLL_SMOOTH:         /* shut up warning */
  6157           break;
  6158         }
  6159     }
  6160   else if (gdk_event_get_scroll_deltas (event, &delta_x, &delta_y))
  6161     {
  6162       if (!mwheel_coalesce_scroll_events)
  6163         {
  6164           inev.ie.kind = ((fabs (delta_x) > fabs (delta_y))
  6165                           ? HORIZ_WHEEL_EVENT
  6166                           : WHEEL_EVENT);
  6167           inev.ie.modifiers |= (inev.ie.kind == HORIZ_WHEEL_EVENT
  6168                                 ? (delta_x >= 0 ? up_modifier : down_modifier)
  6169                                 : (delta_y >= 0 ? down_modifier : up_modifier));
  6170           inev.ie.arg = list3 (Qnil, make_float (-delta_x * 100),
  6171                                make_float (-delta_y * 100));
  6172         }
  6173       else
  6174         {
  6175           dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x += delta_x;
  6176           dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y += delta_y;
  6177           if (dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y >= dpyinfo->scroll.y_per_line)
  6178             {
  6179               int nlines = dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y / dpyinfo->scroll.y_per_line;
  6180               inev.ie.kind = WHEEL_EVENT;
  6181               inev.ie.modifiers |= down_modifier;
  6182               inev.ie.arg = list3 (make_fixnum (nlines),
  6183                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x * 100),
  6184                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y * 100));
  6185               dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y -= dpyinfo->scroll.y_per_line * nlines;
  6186             }
  6187           else if (dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y <= -dpyinfo->scroll.y_per_line)
  6188             {
  6189               int nlines = -dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y / dpyinfo->scroll.y_per_line;
  6190               inev.ie.kind = WHEEL_EVENT;
  6191               inev.ie.modifiers |= up_modifier;
  6192               inev.ie.arg = list3 (make_fixnum (nlines),
  6193                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x * 100),
  6194                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y * 100));
  6195 
  6196               dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y -= -dpyinfo->scroll.y_per_line * nlines;
  6197             }
  6198           else if (dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x >= dpyinfo->scroll.x_per_char
  6199                    || !mwheel_coalesce_scroll_events)
  6200             {
  6201               int nchars = dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x / dpyinfo->scroll.x_per_char;
  6202               inev.ie.kind = HORIZ_WHEEL_EVENT;
  6203               inev.ie.modifiers |= up_modifier;
  6204               inev.ie.arg = list3 (make_fixnum (nchars),
  6205                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x * 100),
  6206                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y * 100));
  6207 
  6208               dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x -= dpyinfo->scroll.x_per_char * nchars;
  6209             }
  6210           else if (dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x <= -dpyinfo->scroll.x_per_char)
  6211             {
  6212               int nchars = -dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x / dpyinfo->scroll.x_per_char;
  6213               inev.ie.kind = HORIZ_WHEEL_EVENT;
  6214               inev.ie.modifiers |= down_modifier;
  6215               inev.ie.arg = list3 (make_fixnum (nchars),
  6216                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x * 100),
  6217                                    make_float (-dpyinfo->scroll.acc_y * 100));
  6218 
  6219               dpyinfo->scroll.acc_x -= -dpyinfo->scroll.x_per_char * nchars;
  6220             }
  6221         }
  6222     }
  6223 
  6224   if (inev.ie.kind != NO_EVENT)
  6225     {
  6226       inev.ie.device
  6227         = pgtk_get_device_for_event (FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f), event);
  6228       evq_enqueue (&inev);
  6229     }
  6230   return TRUE;
  6231 }
  6232 
  6233 
  6234 
  6235 /* C part of drop handling code.
  6236    The Lisp part is in pgtk-dnd.el.  */
  6237 
  6238 static GdkDragAction
  6239 symbol_to_drag_action (Lisp_Object act)
  6240 {
  6241   if (EQ (act, Qcopy))
  6242     return GDK_ACTION_COPY;
  6243 
  6244   if (EQ (act, Qmove))
  6245     return GDK_ACTION_MOVE;
  6246 
  6247   if (EQ (act, Qlink))
  6248     return GDK_ACTION_LINK;
  6249 
  6250   if (EQ (act, Qprivate))
  6251     return GDK_ACTION_PRIVATE;
  6252 
  6253   if (NILP (act))
  6254     return GDK_ACTION_DEFAULT;
  6255 
  6256   signal_error ("Invalid drag acction", act);
  6257 }
  6258 
  6259 static Lisp_Object
  6260 drag_action_to_symbol (GdkDragAction action)
  6261 {
  6262   switch (action)
  6263     {
  6264     case GDK_ACTION_COPY:
  6265       return Qcopy;
  6266 
  6267     case GDK_ACTION_MOVE:
  6268       return Qmove;
  6269 
  6270     case GDK_ACTION_LINK:
  6271       return Qlink;
  6272 
  6273     case GDK_ACTION_PRIVATE:
  6274       return Qprivate;
  6275 
  6276     case GDK_ACTION_DEFAULT:
  6277     default:
  6278       return Qnil;
  6279     }
  6280 }
  6281 
  6282 void
  6283 pgtk_update_drop_status (Lisp_Object action, Lisp_Object event_time)
  6284 {
  6285   guint32 time;
  6286 
  6287   CONS_TO_INTEGER (event_time, guint32, time);
  6288 
  6289   if (!current_drop_context || time < current_drop_time)
  6290     return;
  6291 
  6292   gdk_drag_status (current_drop_context,
  6293                    symbol_to_drag_action (action),
  6294                    time);
  6295 }
  6296 
  6297 void
  6298 pgtk_finish_drop (Lisp_Object success, Lisp_Object event_time,
  6299                   Lisp_Object del)
  6300 {
  6301   guint32 time;
  6302 
  6303   CONS_TO_INTEGER (event_time, guint32, time);
  6304 
  6305   if (!current_drop_context || time < current_drop_time)
  6306     return;
  6307 
  6308   gtk_drag_finish (current_drop_context, !NILP (success),
  6309                    !NILP (del), time);
  6310 
  6311   if (current_drop_context_drop)
  6312     g_clear_pointer (&current_drop_context,
  6313                      g_object_unref);
  6314 }
  6315 
  6316 static void
  6317 drag_leave (GtkWidget *widget, GdkDragContext *context,
  6318             guint time, gpointer user_data)
  6319 {
  6320   struct frame *f;
  6321   union buffered_input_event inev;
  6322 
  6323   f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  6324 
  6325   if (current_drop_context)
  6326     {
  6327       if (current_drop_context_drop)
  6328         gtk_drag_finish (current_drop_context,
  6329                          FALSE, FALSE, current_drop_time);
  6330 
  6331       g_clear_pointer (&current_drop_context,
  6332                        g_object_unref);
  6333     }
  6334 
  6335   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  6336 
  6337   inev.ie.kind = DRAG_N_DROP_EVENT;
  6338   inev.ie.modifiers = 0;
  6339   inev.ie.arg = Qnil;
  6340   inev.ie.timestamp = time;
  6341 
  6342   XSETINT (inev.ie.x, 0);
  6343   XSETINT (inev.ie.y, 0);
  6344   XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  6345 
  6346   evq_enqueue (&inev);
  6347 }
  6348 
  6349 static gboolean
  6350 drag_motion (GtkWidget *widget, GdkDragContext *context,
  6351              gint x, gint y, guint time)
  6352 
  6353 {
  6354   struct frame *f;
  6355   union buffered_input_event inev;
  6356   GdkAtom name;
  6357   GdkDragAction suggestion;
  6358 
  6359   f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  6360 
  6361   if (!f)
  6362     return FALSE;
  6363 
  6364   if (current_drop_context)
  6365     {
  6366       if (current_drop_context_drop)
  6367         gtk_drag_finish (current_drop_context,
  6368                          FALSE, FALSE, current_drop_time);
  6369 
  6370       g_clear_pointer (&current_drop_context,
  6371                        g_object_unref);
  6372     }
  6373 
  6374   current_drop_context = g_object_ref (context);
  6375   current_drop_time = time;
  6376   current_drop_context_drop = false;
  6377 
  6378   name = gdk_drag_get_selection (context);
  6379   suggestion = gdk_drag_context_get_suggested_action (context);
  6380 
  6381   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  6382 
  6383   inev.ie.kind = DRAG_N_DROP_EVENT;
  6384   inev.ie.modifiers = 0;
  6385   inev.ie.arg = list4 (Qlambda, intern (gdk_atom_name (name)),
  6386                        make_uint (time),
  6387                        drag_action_to_symbol (suggestion));
  6388   inev.ie.timestamp = time;
  6389 
  6390   XSETINT (inev.ie.x, x);
  6391   XSETINT (inev.ie.y, y);
  6392   XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  6393 
  6394   evq_enqueue (&inev);
  6395 
  6396   return TRUE;
  6397 }
  6398 
  6399 static gboolean
  6400 drag_drop (GtkWidget *widget, GdkDragContext *context,
  6401            int x, int y, guint time, gpointer user_data)
  6402 {
  6403   struct frame *f;
  6404   union buffered_input_event inev;
  6405   GdkAtom name;
  6406   GdkDragAction selected_action;
  6407 
  6408   f = pgtk_any_window_to_frame (gtk_widget_get_window (widget));
  6409 
  6410   if (!f)
  6411     return FALSE;
  6412 
  6413   if (current_drop_context)
  6414     {
  6415       if (current_drop_context_drop)
  6416         gtk_drag_finish (current_drop_context,
  6417                          FALSE, FALSE, current_drop_time);
  6418 
  6419       g_clear_pointer (&current_drop_context,
  6420                        g_object_unref);
  6421     }
  6422 
  6423   current_drop_context = g_object_ref (context);
  6424   current_drop_time = time;
  6425   current_drop_context_drop = true;
  6426 
  6427   name = gdk_drag_get_selection (context);
  6428   selected_action = gdk_drag_context_get_selected_action (context);
  6429 
  6430   EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  6431 
  6432   inev.ie.kind = DRAG_N_DROP_EVENT;
  6433   inev.ie.modifiers = 0;
  6434   inev.ie.arg = list4 (Qquote, intern (gdk_atom_name (name)),
  6435                        make_uint (time),
  6436                        drag_action_to_symbol (selected_action));
  6437   inev.ie.timestamp = time;
  6438 
  6439   XSETINT (inev.ie.x, x);
  6440   XSETINT (inev.ie.y, y);
  6441   XSETFRAME (inev.ie.frame_or_window, f);
  6442 
  6443   evq_enqueue (&inev);
  6444 
  6445   return TRUE;
  6446 }

  6464 void

  6466 {

  6468     {
  6469       g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "draw",
  6470                         G_CALLBACK (pgtk_handle_draw), NULL);

  6472     }

  6474   gtk_drag_dest_set (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f), 0, NULL, 0,

  6477 
  6478   if (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f))
  6479     {
  6480       g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f)),
  6481                         "window-state-event", G_CALLBACK (window_state_event),
  6482                         NULL);

  6484                         G_CALLBACK (delete_event), NULL);
  6485       g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f)), "event",
  6486                         G_CALLBACK (pgtk_handle_event), NULL);
  6487       g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_OUTER_WIDGET (f)), "configure-event",
  6488                         G_CALLBACK (configure_event), NULL);
  6489     }
  6490 
  6491   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "map-event",
  6492                     G_CALLBACK (map_event), NULL);
  6493   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "size-allocate",
  6494                     G_CALLBACK (size_allocate), f);
  6495   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "key-press-event",
  6496                     G_CALLBACK (key_press_event), NULL);
  6497   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "key-release-event",
  6498                     G_CALLBACK (key_release_event), NULL);

  6500                     G_CALLBACK (focus_in_event), NULL);
  6501   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "focus-out-event",
  6502                     G_CALLBACK (focus_out_event), NULL);
  6503   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "enter-notify-event",
  6504                     G_CALLBACK (enter_notify_event), NULL);
  6505   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "leave-notify-event",
  6506                     G_CALLBACK (leave_notify_event), NULL);

  6508                     G_CALLBACK (motion_notify_event), NULL);

  6510                     G_CALLBACK (button_event), NULL);
  6511   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "button-release-event",

  6522                     G_CALLBACK (drag_drop), NULL);
  6523   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "draw",
  6524                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_handle_draw), NULL);

  6526                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_selection_event), NULL);

  6530                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_selection_event), NULL);

  6532                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_selection_event), NULL);
  6533   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)), "event",
  6534                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_handle_event), NULL);
  6535 }
