  6537 static void
  6538 my_log_handler (const gchar * log_domain, GLogLevelFlags log_level,
  6539                 const gchar * msg, gpointer user_data)
  6540 {
  6541   if (!strstr (msg, "g_set_prgname"))
  6542     fprintf (stderr, "%s-WARNING **: %s", log_domain, msg);
  6543 }
  6544 
  6545 /* Test whether two display-name strings agree up to the dot that separates
  6546    the screen number from the server number.  */
  6547 static bool
  6548 same_x_server (const char *name1, const char *name2)
  6549 {
  6550   bool seen_colon = false;
  6551   Lisp_Object sysname = Fsystem_name ();
  6552   const char *system_name = SSDATA (sysname);
  6553   ptrdiff_t system_name_length = SBYTES (sysname);
  6554   ptrdiff_t length_until_period = 0;
  6555 
  6556   while (system_name[length_until_period] != 0
  6557          && system_name[length_until_period] != '.')
  6558     length_until_period++;
  6559 
  6560   /* Treat `unix' like an empty host name.  */
  6561   if (!strncmp (name1, "unix:", 5))
  6562     name1 += 4;
  6563   if (!strncmp (name2, "unix:", 5))
  6564     name2 += 4;
  6565   /* Treat this host's name like an empty host name.  */
  6566   if (!strncmp (name1, system_name, system_name_length)
  6567       && name1[system_name_length] == ':')
  6568     name1 += system_name_length;
  6569   if (!strncmp (name2, system_name, system_name_length)
  6570       && name2[system_name_length] == ':')
  6571     name2 += system_name_length;
  6572   /* Treat this host's domainless name like an empty host name.  */
  6573   if (!strncmp (name1, system_name, length_until_period)
  6574       && name1[length_until_period] == ':')
  6575     name1 += length_until_period;
  6576   if (!strncmp (name2, system_name, length_until_period)
  6577       && name2[length_until_period] == ':')
  6578     name2 += length_until_period;
  6579 
  6580   for (; *name1 != '\0' && *name1 == *name2; name1++, name2++)
  6581     {
  6582       if (*name1 == ':')
  6583         seen_colon = true;
  6584       if (seen_colon && *name1 == '.')
  6585         return true;
  6586     }
  6587   return (seen_colon
  6588           && (*name1 == '.' || *name1 == '\0')
  6589           && (*name2 == '.' || *name2 == '\0'));
  6590 }
  6591 
  6592 static struct frame *
  6593 pgtk_find_selection_owner (GdkWindow *window)
  6594 {
  6595   Lisp_Object tail, tem;
  6596   struct frame *f;
  6597 
  6598   FOR_EACH_FRAME (tail, tem)
  6599     {
  6600       f = XFRAME (tem);
  6601 
  6602       if (FRAME_PGTK_P (f)
  6603           && (FRAME_GDK_WINDOW (f) == window))
  6604         return f;
  6605     }
  6606 
  6607   return NULL;
  6608 }
  6609 
  6610 static gboolean
  6611 pgtk_selection_event (GtkWidget *widget, GdkEvent *event,
  6612                       gpointer user_data)
  6613 {
  6614   struct frame *f;
  6615   union buffered_input_event inev;
  6616 
  6617   if (event->type == GDK_PROPERTY_NOTIFY)
  6618     pgtk_handle_property_notify (&event->property);
  6619   else if (event->type == GDK_SELECTION_CLEAR
  6620            || event->type == GDK_SELECTION_REQUEST)
  6621     {
  6622       f = pgtk_find_selection_owner (event->selection.window);
  6623 
  6624       if (f)
  6625         {
  6626           EVENT_INIT (inev.ie);
  6627 
  6628           inev.sie.kind = (event->type == GDK_SELECTION_CLEAR
  6629                            ? SELECTION_CLEAR_EVENT
  6630                            : SELECTION_REQUEST_EVENT);
  6631 
  6632           SELECTION_EVENT_DPYINFO (&inev.sie) = FRAME_DISPLAY_INFO (f);
  6633           SELECTION_EVENT_SELECTION (&inev.sie) = event->selection.selection;
  6634           SELECTION_EVENT_TIME (&inev.sie) = event->selection.time;
  6635 
  6636           if (event->type == GDK_SELECTION_REQUEST)
  6637             {
  6638               /* FIXME: when does GDK destroy the requestor GdkWindow
  6639                  object?
  6640 
  6641                  It would make sense to wait for the transfer to
  6642                  complete.  But I don't know if GDK actually does
  6643                  that.  */
  6644               SELECTION_EVENT_REQUESTOR (&inev.sie) = event->selection.requestor;
  6645               SELECTION_EVENT_TARGET (&inev.sie) = event->selection.target;
  6646               SELECTION_EVENT_PROPERTY (&inev.sie) = event->selection.property;
  6647             }
  6648 
  6649           evq_enqueue (&inev);
  6650           return TRUE;
  6651         }
  6652     }
  6653   else if (event->type == GDK_SELECTION_NOTIFY)
  6654     pgtk_handle_selection_notify (&event->selection);
  6655 
  6656   return FALSE;
  6657 }
  6658 
  6659 /* Display a warning message if the PGTK port is being used under X;
  6660    that is not supported.  */
  6661 
  6662 static void
  6663 pgtk_display_x_warning (GdkDisplay *display)
  6664 {
  6665   GtkWidget *dialog_widget, *label, *content_area;
  6666   GtkDialog *dialog;
  6667   GtkWindow *window;
  6668   GdkScreen *screen;
  6669 
  6670   /* Do this instead of GDK_IS_X11_DISPLAY because the GDK X header
  6671      pulls in Xlib, which conflicts with definitions in pgtkgui.h.  */
  6672   if (strcmp (G_OBJECT_TYPE_NAME (display),
  6673               "GdkX11Display"))
  6674     return;
  6675 
  6676   dialog_widget = gtk_dialog_new ();
  6677   dialog = GTK_DIALOG (dialog_widget);
  6678   window = GTK_WINDOW (dialog_widget);
  6679   screen = gdk_display_get_default_screen (display);
  6680   content_area = gtk_dialog_get_content_area (dialog);
  6681 
  6682   gtk_window_set_title (window, "Warning");
  6683   gtk_window_set_screen (window, screen);
  6684 
  6685   label = gtk_label_new ("You are trying to run Emacs configured with"
  6686                           " the \"pure-GTK\" interface under the X Window"
  6687                           " System.  That configuration is unsupported and"
  6688                           " will lead to sporadic crashes during transfer of"
  6689                           " large selection data.  It will also lead to"
  6690                           " various problems with keyboard input.");
  6691   gtk_label_set_line_wrap (GTK_LABEL (label), TRUE);
  6692   gtk_container_add (GTK_CONTAINER (content_area), label);
  6693   gtk_widget_show (label);
  6694   gtk_widget_show (dialog_widget);
  6695 }
  6696 
  6697 /* Open a connection to X display DISPLAY_NAME, and return
  6698    the structure that describes the open display.
  6699    If we cannot contact the display, return null.  */
  6700 
  6701 struct pgtk_display_info *
  6702 pgtk_term_init (Lisp_Object display_name, char *resource_name)
  6703 {
  6704   GdkDisplay *dpy;
  6705   struct terminal *terminal;
  6706   struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo;
  6707   static int x_initialized = 0;
  6708   static unsigned x_display_id = 0;
  6709   static char *initial_display = NULL;
  6710   char *dpy_name;
  6711   static void *handle = NULL;
  6712   Lisp_Object lisp_dpy_name = Qnil;
  6713   GdkScreen *gscr;
  6714   gdouble dpi;
  6715 
  6716   block_input ();
  6717 
  6718   if (!x_initialized)
  6719     {
  6720       any_help_event_p = false;
  6721 
  6722       Fset_input_interrupt_mode (Qt);
  6723       baud_rate = 19200;
  6724 
  6725 #ifdef USE_CAIRO
  6726       gui_init_fringe (&pgtk_redisplay_interface);
  6727 #endif
  6728 
  6729       ++x_initialized;
  6730     }
  6731 
  6732   dpy_name = SSDATA (display_name);
  6733   if (strlen (dpy_name) == 0 && initial_display != NULL)
  6734     dpy_name = initial_display;
  6735   lisp_dpy_name = build_string (dpy_name);
  6736 
  6737   {
  6738 #define NUM_ARGV 10
  6739     int argc;
  6740     char *argv[NUM_ARGV];
  6741     char **argv2 = argv;
  6742     guint id;
  6743 
  6744     if (x_initialized++ > 1)
  6745       {
  6746         xg_display_open (dpy_name, &dpy);
  6747       }
  6748     else
  6749       {
  6750         static char display_opt[] = "--display";
  6751         static char name_opt[] = "--name";
  6752 
  6753         for (argc = 0; argc < NUM_ARGV; ++argc)
  6754           argv[argc] = 0;
  6755 
  6756         argc = 0;
  6757         argv[argc++] = initial_argv[0];
  6758 
  6759         if (strlen (dpy_name) != 0)
  6760           {
  6761             argv[argc++] = display_opt;
  6762             argv[argc++] = dpy_name;
  6763           }
  6764 
  6765         argv[argc++] = name_opt;
  6766         argv[argc++] = resource_name;
  6767 
  6768         /* Work around GLib bug that outputs a faulty warning. See
  6769            https://bugzilla.gnome.org/show_bug.cgi?id=563627.  */
  6770         id = g_log_set_handler ("GLib", G_LOG_LEVEL_WARNING | G_LOG_FLAG_FATAL
  6771                                 | G_LOG_FLAG_RECURSION, my_log_handler, NULL);
  6772 
  6773         /* gtk_init does set_locale.  Fix locale before and after.  */
  6774         fixup_locale ();
  6775         unrequest_sigio ();     /* See comment in x_display_ok.  */
  6776         gtk_init (&argc, &argv2);
  6777         request_sigio ();
  6778         fixup_locale ();
  6779 
  6780 
  6781         g_log_remove_handler ("GLib", id);
  6782 
  6783         xg_initialize ();
  6784 
  6785         dpy = DEFAULT_GDK_DISPLAY ();
  6786 
  6787         initial_display = g_strdup (gdk_display_get_name (dpy));
  6788         dpy_name = initial_display;
  6789         lisp_dpy_name = build_string (dpy_name);
  6790       }
  6791   }
  6792 
  6793   /* Detect failure.  */
  6794   if (dpy == 0)
  6795     {
  6796       unblock_input ();
  6797       return 0;
  6798     }
  6799 
  6800   /* If the PGTK port is being used under X, complain very loudly, as
  6801      that isn't supported.  */
  6802   pgtk_display_x_warning (dpy);
  6803 
  6804   dpyinfo = xzalloc (sizeof *dpyinfo);
  6805   pgtk_initialize_display_info (dpyinfo);
  6806   terminal = pgtk_create_terminal (dpyinfo);
  6807 
  6808   {
  6809     struct pgtk_display_info *share;
  6810 
  6811     for (share = x_display_list; share; share = share->next)
  6812       if (same_x_server (SSDATA (XCAR (share->name_list_element)), dpy_name))
  6813         break;
  6814     if (share)
  6815       terminal->kboard = share->terminal->kboard;
  6816     else
  6817       {
  6818         terminal->kboard = allocate_kboard (Qpgtk);
  6819 
  6820         /* Don't let the initial kboard remain current longer than necessary.
  6821            That would cause problems if a file loaded on startup tries to
  6822            prompt in the mini-buffer.  */
  6823         if (current_kboard == initial_kboard)
  6824           current_kboard = terminal->kboard;
  6825       }
  6826     terminal->kboard->reference_count++;
  6827   }
  6828 
  6829   /* Put this display on the chain.  */
  6830   dpyinfo->next = x_display_list;
  6831   x_display_list = dpyinfo;
  6832 
  6833   dpyinfo->name_list_element = Fcons (lisp_dpy_name, Qnil);
  6834   dpyinfo->gdpy = dpy;
  6835 
  6836   /* https://lists.gnu.org/r/emacs-devel/2015-11/msg00194.html  */
  6837   dpyinfo->smallest_font_height = 1;
  6838   dpyinfo->smallest_char_width = 1;
  6839 
  6840   /* Set the name of the terminal. */
  6841   terminal->name = xlispstrdup (lisp_dpy_name);
  6842 
  6843   Lisp_Object system_name = Fsystem_name ();
  6844   ptrdiff_t nbytes;
  6845   if (INT_ADD_WRAPV (SBYTES (Vinvocation_name), SBYTES (system_name) + 2,
  6846                      &nbytes))
  6847     memory_full (SIZE_MAX);
  6848   dpyinfo->x_id = ++x_display_id;
  6849   dpyinfo->x_id_name = xmalloc (nbytes);
  6850   char *nametail = lispstpcpy (dpyinfo->x_id_name, Vinvocation_name);
  6851   *nametail++ = '@';
  6852   lispstpcpy (nametail, system_name);
  6853 
  6854   /* Get the scroll bar cursor.  */
  6855   /* We must create a GTK cursor, it is required for GTK widgets.  */
  6856   dpyinfo->xg_cursor = xg_create_default_cursor (dpyinfo->gdpy);
  6857 
  6858   dpyinfo->vertical_scroll_bar_cursor
  6859     = gdk_cursor_new_for_display (dpyinfo->gdpy, GDK_SB_V_DOUBLE_ARROW);
  6860 
  6861   dpyinfo->horizontal_scroll_bar_cursor
  6862     = gdk_cursor_new_for_display (dpyinfo->gdpy, GDK_SB_H_DOUBLE_ARROW);
  6863 
  6864   dpyinfo->icon_bitmap_id = -1;
  6865 
  6866   reset_mouse_highlight (&dpyinfo->mouse_highlight);
  6867 
  6868   gscr = gdk_display_get_default_screen (dpyinfo->gdpy);
  6869   dpi = gdk_screen_get_resolution (gscr);
  6870 
  6871   if (dpi < 0)
  6872     dpi = 96.0;
  6873 
  6874   dpyinfo->resx = dpi;
  6875   dpyinfo->resy = dpi;
  6876 
  6877   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (gscr), "monitors-changed",
  6878                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_monitors_changed_cb),
  6879                     terminal);
  6880 
  6881   /* Set up scrolling increments.  */
  6882   dpyinfo->scroll.x_per_char = 1;
  6883   dpyinfo->scroll.y_per_line = 1;
  6884 
  6885   dpyinfo->connection = -1;
  6886 
  6887   if (!handle)
  6888     handle = dlopen (NULL, RTLD_LAZY);
  6889 
  6890 #ifdef GDK_WINDOWING_X11
  6891   if (!strcmp (G_OBJECT_TYPE_NAME (dpy), "GdkX11Display") && handle)
  6892     {
  6893       void *(*gdk_x11_display_get_xdisplay) (GdkDisplay *)
  6894         = dlsym (handle, "gdk_x11_display_get_xdisplay");
  6895       int (*x_connection_number) (void *)
  6896         = dlsym (handle, "XConnectionNumber");
  6897 
  6898       if (x_connection_number
  6899           && gdk_x11_display_get_xdisplay)
  6900         dpyinfo->connection
  6901           = x_connection_number (gdk_x11_display_get_xdisplay (dpy));
  6902     }
  6903 #endif
  6904 
  6905 #ifdef GDK_WINDOWING_WAYLAND
  6906   if (GDK_IS_WAYLAND_DISPLAY (dpy) && handle)
  6907     {
  6908       struct wl_display *wl_dpy = gdk_wayland_display_get_wl_display (dpy);
  6909       int (*display_get_fd) (struct wl_display *)
  6910         = dlsym (handle, "wl_display_get_fd");
  6911 
  6912       if (display_get_fd)
  6913         dpyinfo->connection = display_get_fd (wl_dpy);
  6914     }
  6915 #endif
  6916 
  6917   if (dpyinfo->connection >= 0)
  6918     {
  6919       add_keyboard_wait_descriptor (dpyinfo->connection);
  6920 #ifdef F_SETOWN
  6921       fcntl (dpyinfo->connection, F_SETOWN, getpid ());
  6922 #endif /* ! defined (F_SETOWN) */
  6923 
  6924       if (interrupt_input)
  6925         init_sigio (dpyinfo->connection);
  6926     }
  6927 
  6928   dpyinfo->invisible_cursor
  6929     = gdk_cursor_new_for_display (dpyinfo->gdpy, GDK_BLANK_CURSOR);
  6930 
  6931   xsettings_initialize (dpyinfo);
  6932 
  6933   pgtk_im_init (dpyinfo);
  6934 
  6935   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (dpyinfo->gdpy), "seat-added",
  6936                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_seat_added_cb), dpyinfo);
  6937   g_signal_connect (G_OBJECT (dpyinfo->gdpy), "seat-removed",
  6938                     G_CALLBACK (pgtk_seat_removed_cb), dpyinfo);
  6939   pgtk_enumerate_devices (dpyinfo, true);
  6940 
  6941   unblock_input ();
  6942 
  6943   return dpyinfo;
  6944 }
  6945 
  6946 /* Get rid of display DPYINFO, deleting all frames on it,
  6947    and without sending any more commands to the X server.  */
  6948 
  6949 static void
  6950 pgtk_delete_display (struct pgtk_display_info *dpyinfo)
  6951 {
  6952   struct terminal *t;
  6953 
  6954   /* Close all frames and delete the generic struct terminal for this
  6955      X display.  */
  6956   for (t = terminal_list; t; t = t->next_terminal)
  6957     if (t->type == output_pgtk && t->display_info.pgtk == dpyinfo)
  6958       {
  6959         delete_terminal (t);
  6960         break;
  6961       }
  6962 
  6963   if (x_display_list == dpyinfo)
  6964     x_display_list = dpyinfo->next;
  6965   else
  6966     {
  6967       struct pgtk_display_info *tail;
  6968 
  6969       for (tail = x_display_list; tail; tail = tail->next)
  6970         if (tail->next == dpyinfo)
  6971           tail->next = tail->next->next;
  6972     }
  6973 
  6974   pgtk_free_devices (dpyinfo);
  6975   xfree (dpyinfo);
  6976 }
  6977 
  6978 char *
  6979 pgtk_xlfd_to_fontname (const char *xlfd)
  6980 /* --------------------------------------------------------------------------
  6981     Convert an X font name (XLFD) to an Gtk font name.
  6982     Only family is used.
  6983     The string returned is temporarily allocated.
  6984    -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */
  6985 {
  6986   char *name = xmalloc (180);
  6987 
  6988   if (!strncmp (xlfd, "--", 2))
  6989     {
  6990       if (sscanf (xlfd, "--%179[^-]-", name) != 1)
  6991         name[0] = '\0';
  6992     }
  6993   else
  6994     {
  6995       if (sscanf (xlfd, "-%*[^-]-%179[^-]-", name) != 1)
  6996         name[0] = '\0';
  6997     }
  6998 
  6999   /* stopgap for malformed XLFD input */
  7000   if (strlen (name) == 0)
  7001     strcpy (name, "Monospace");
  7002 
  7003   return name;
  7004 }
  7005 
  7006 bool
  7007 pgtk_defined_color (struct frame *f, const char *name,
  7008                     Emacs_Color *color_def, bool alloc,
  7009                     bool makeIndex)
  7010 /* --------------------------------------------------------------------------
  7011          Return true if named color found, and set color_def rgb accordingly.
  7012          If makeIndex and alloc are nonzero put the color in the color_table,
  7013          and set color_def pixel to the resulting index.
  7014          If makeIndex is zero, set color_def pixel to ARGB.
  7015          Return false if not found
  7016    -------------------------------------------------------------------------- */
  7017 {
  7018   int r;
  7019 
  7020   block_input ();
  7021   r = xg_check_special_colors (f, name, color_def);
  7022   if (!r)
  7023     r = pgtk_parse_color (f, name, color_def);
  7024   unblock_input ();
  7025   return r;
  7026 }
  7027 
  7028 /* On frame F, translate the color name to RGB values.  Use cached
  7029    information, if possible.
  7030 
  7031    Note that there is currently no way to clean old entries out of the
  7032    cache.  However, it is limited to names in the server's database,
  7033    and names we've actually looked up; list-colors-display is probably
  7034    the most color-intensive case we're likely to hit.  */
  7035 
  7036 int
  7037 pgtk_parse_color (struct frame *f, const char *color_name,
  7038                   Emacs_Color * color)
  7039 {
  7040   GdkRGBA rgba;
  7041   if (gdk_rgba_parse (&rgba, color_name))
  7042     {
  7043       color->red = rgba.red * 65535;
  7044       color->green = rgba.green * 65535;
  7045       color->blue = rgba.blue * 65535;
  7046       color->pixel = ((color->red >> 8) << 16
  7047                       | (color->green >> 8) << 8
  7048                       | (color->blue >> 8) << 0);
  7049       return 1;
  7050     }
  7051   return 0;
  7052 }
  7053 
  7054 /* On frame F, translate pixel colors to RGB values for the NCOLORS
  7055    colors in COLORS.  On W32, we no longer try to map colors to
  7056    a palette.  */
  7057 void
  7058 pgtk_query_colors (struct frame *f, Emacs_Color * colors, int ncolors)
  7059 {
  7060   int i;
  7061 
  7062   for (i = 0; i < ncolors; i++)
  7063     {
  7064       unsigned long pixel = colors[i].pixel;
  7065       /* Convert to a 16 bit value in range 0 - 0xffff. */
  7066 #define GetRValue(p) (((p) >> 16) & 0xff)
  7067 #define GetGValue(p) (((p) >> 8) & 0xff)
  7068 #define GetBValue(p) (((p) >> 0) & 0xff)
  7069       colors[i].red = GetRValue (pixel) * 257;
  7070       colors[i].green = GetGValue (pixel) * 257;
  7071       colors[i].blue = GetBValue (pixel) * 257;
  7072     }
  7073 }
  7074 
  7075 void
  7076 pgtk_query_color (struct frame *f, Emacs_Color * color)
  7077 {
  7078   pgtk_query_colors (f, color, 1);
  7079 }
  7080 
  7081 void
  7082 pgtk_clear_area (struct frame *f, int x, int y, int width, int height)
  7083 {
  7084   cairo_t *cr;
  7085 
  7086   eassert (width > 0 && height > 0);
  7087 
  7088   cr = pgtk_begin_cr_clip (f);
  7089   pgtk_set_cr_source_with_color (f, FRAME_X_OUTPUT (f)->background_color,
  7090                                  true);
  7091   cairo_rectangle (cr, x, y, width, height);
  7092   cairo_fill (cr);
  7093   pgtk_end_cr_clip (f);
  7094 }

  7096 
  7097 void
  7098 syms_of_pgtkterm (void)
  7099 {
  7100   DEFSYM (Qmodifier_value, "modifier-value");
  7101   DEFSYM (Qalt, "alt");
  7102   DEFSYM (Qhyper, "hyper");
  7103   DEFSYM (Qmeta, "meta");
  7104   DEFSYM (Qsuper, "super");
  7105   DEFSYM (Qcontrol, "control");
  7106   DEFSYM (QUTF8_STRING, "UTF8_STRING");
  7107 
  7108   DEFSYM (Qfile, "file");
  7109   DEFSYM (Qurl, "url");
  7110 
  7111   DEFSYM (Qlatin_1, "latin-1");
  7112 
  7113   xg_default_icon_file
  7114     = build_pure_c_string ("icons/hicolor/scalable/apps/emacs.svg");
  7115   staticpro (&xg_default_icon_file);
  7116 
  7117   DEFSYM (Qx_gtk_map_stock, "x-gtk-map-stock");
  7118 
  7119   DEFSYM (Qcopy, "copy");
  7120   DEFSYM (Qmove, "move");
  7121   DEFSYM (Qlink, "link");
  7122   DEFSYM (Qprivate, "private");
  7123 
  7124 
  7125   Fput (Qalt, Qmodifier_value, make_fixnum (alt_modifier));
  7126   Fput (Qhyper, Qmodifier_value, make_fixnum (hyper_modifier));
  7127   Fput (Qmeta, Qmodifier_value, make_fixnum (meta_modifier));
  7128   Fput (Qsuper, Qmodifier_value, make_fixnum (super_modifier));
  7129   Fput (Qcontrol, Qmodifier_value, make_fixnum (ctrl_modifier));
  7130 
  7131   DEFVAR_LISP ("x-ctrl-keysym", Vx_ctrl_keysym,
  7132                doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7133   Vx_ctrl_keysym = Qnil;
  7134 
  7135   DEFVAR_LISP ("x-alt-keysym", Vx_alt_keysym,
  7136                doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7137   Vx_alt_keysym = Qnil;
  7138 
  7139   DEFVAR_LISP ("x-hyper-keysym", Vx_hyper_keysym,
  7140                doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7141   Vx_hyper_keysym = Qnil;
  7142 
  7143   DEFVAR_LISP ("x-meta-keysym", Vx_meta_keysym,
  7144                doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7145   Vx_meta_keysym = Qnil;
  7146 
  7147   DEFVAR_LISP ("x-super-keysym", Vx_super_keysym,
  7148                doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7149   Vx_super_keysym = Qnil;
  7150 
  7151   DEFVAR_BOOL ("x-use-underline-position-properties",
  7152                x_use_underline_position_properties,
  7153      doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7154   x_use_underline_position_properties = 1;
  7155 
  7156   DEFVAR_BOOL ("x-underline-at-descent-line",
  7157                x_underline_at_descent_line,
  7158      doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7159   x_underline_at_descent_line = 0;
  7160 
  7161   DEFVAR_LISP ("x-toolkit-scroll-bars", Vx_toolkit_scroll_bars,
  7162      doc: /* SKIP: real doc in xterm.c.  */);
  7163   Vx_toolkit_scroll_bars = intern_c_string ("gtk");
  7164 
  7165   DEFVAR_LISP ("pgtk-wait-for-event-timeout", Vpgtk_wait_for_event_timeout,
  7166                doc: /* How long to wait for GTK events.
  7167 
  7168 Emacs will wait up to this many seconds to receive some GTK events
  7169 after making changes which affect the state of the graphical
  7170 interface.  Under some window managers this can take an indefinite
  7171 amount of time, so it is important to limit the wait.
  7172 
  7173 If set to a non-float value, there will be no wait at all.  */);
  7174   Vpgtk_wait_for_event_timeout = make_float (0.1);
  7175 
  7176   DEFVAR_LISP ("pgtk-keysym-table", Vpgtk_keysym_table,
  7177     doc: /* Hash table of character codes indexed by X keysym codes.  */);
  7178   Vpgtk_keysym_table = make_hash_table (hashtest_eql, 900, DEFAULT_REHASH_SIZE,
  7179                                         DEFAULT_REHASH_THRESHOLD, Qnil, false);
  7180 
  7181   window_being_scrolled = Qnil;
  7182   staticpro (&window_being_scrolled);
  7183 
  7184   /* Tell Emacs about this window system.  */
  7185   Fprovide (Qpgtk, Qnil);
  7186 }
  7187 
  7188 /* Cairo does not allow resizing a surface/context after it is
  7189    created, so we need to trash the old context, create a new context
  7190    on the next cr_clip_begin with the new dimensions and request a
  7191    re-draw.
  7192 
  7193    This will leave the active context available to present on screen
  7194    until a redrawn frame is completed.  */
  7195 void
  7196 pgtk_cr_update_surface_desired_size (struct frame *f, int width, int height, bool force)
  7197 {
  7198   if (FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_WIDTH (f) != width
  7199       || FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_HEIGHT (f) != height
  7200       || force)
  7201     {
  7202       pgtk_cr_destroy_frame_context (f);
  7203       FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_WIDTH (f) = width;
  7204       FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_HEIGHT (f) = height;
  7205       SET_FRAME_GARBAGED (f);
  7206     }
  7207 }
  7208 
  7209 
  7210 cairo_t *
  7211 pgtk_begin_cr_clip (struct frame *f)
  7212 {
  7213   cairo_t *cr = FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f);
  7214 
  7215   if (!cr)
  7216     {
  7217       cairo_surface_t *surface
  7218         = gdk_window_create_similar_surface (gtk_widget_get_window
  7219                                              (FRAME_GTK_WIDGET (f)),
  7220                                              CAIRO_CONTENT_COLOR_ALPHA,
  7221                                              FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_WIDTH (f),
  7222                                              FRAME_CR_SURFACE_DESIRED_HEIGHT
  7223                                              (f));
  7224 
  7225       cr = FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f) = cairo_create (surface);
  7226       cairo_surface_destroy (surface);
  7227     }
  7228 
  7229   cairo_save (cr);
  7230 
  7231   return cr;
  7232 }
  7233 
  7234 void
  7235 pgtk_end_cr_clip (struct frame *f)
  7236 {
  7237   cairo_restore (FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f));
  7238 }
  7239 
  7240 void
  7241 pgtk_set_cr_source_with_gc_foreground (struct frame *f, Emacs_GC *gc,
  7242                                        bool respects_alpha_background)
  7243 {
  7244   pgtk_set_cr_source_with_color (f, gc->foreground,
  7245                                  respects_alpha_background);
  7246 }
  7247 
  7248 void
  7249 pgtk_set_cr_source_with_gc_background (struct frame *f, Emacs_GC *gc,
  7250                                        bool respects_alpha_background)
  7251 {
  7252   pgtk_set_cr_source_with_color (f, gc->background,
  7253                                  respects_alpha_background);
  7254 }
  7255 
  7256 void
  7257 pgtk_set_cr_source_with_color (struct frame *f, unsigned long color,
  7258                                bool respects_alpha_background)
  7259 {
  7260   Emacs_Color col;
  7261   col.pixel = color;
  7262   pgtk_query_color (f, &col);
  7263 
  7264   if (!respects_alpha_background)
  7265     {
  7266       cairo_set_source_rgb (FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f), col.red / 65535.0,
  7267                             col.green / 65535.0, col.blue / 65535.0);
  7268       cairo_set_operator (FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f), CAIRO_OPERATOR_OVER);
  7269     }
  7270   else
  7271     {
  7272       cairo_set_source_rgba (FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f), col.red / 65535.0,
  7273                              col.green / 65535.0, col.blue / 65535.0,
  7274                              f->alpha_background);
  7275       cairo_set_operator (FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f), CAIRO_OPERATOR_SOURCE);
  7276     }
  7277 }
  7278 
  7279 void
  7280 pgtk_cr_draw_frame (cairo_t * cr, struct frame *f)
  7281 {
  7282   cairo_set_source_surface (cr, FRAME_CR_SURFACE (f), 0, 0);
  7283   cairo_paint (cr);
  7284 }
  7285 
  7286 static cairo_status_t
  7287 pgtk_cr_accumulate_data (void *closure, const unsigned char *data,
  7288                          unsigned int length)
  7289 {
  7290   Lisp_Object *acc = (Lisp_Object *) closure;
  7291 
  7292   *acc = Fcons (make_unibyte_string ((char const *) data, length), *acc);
  7293 
  7294   return CAIRO_STATUS_SUCCESS;
  7295 }
  7296 
  7297 void
  7298 pgtk_cr_destroy_frame_context (struct frame *f)
  7299 {
  7300   if (FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f) != NULL)
  7301     {
  7302       cairo_destroy (FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f));
  7303       FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f) = NULL;
  7304     }
  7305 }
  7306 
  7307 static void
  7308 pgtk_cr_destroy (void *cr)
  7309 {
  7310   block_input ();
  7311   cairo_destroy (cr);
  7312   unblock_input ();
  7313 }
  7314 
  7315 Lisp_Object
  7316 pgtk_cr_export_frames (Lisp_Object frames, cairo_surface_type_t surface_type)
  7317 {
  7318   struct frame *f;
  7319   cairo_surface_t *surface;
  7320   cairo_t *cr;
  7321   int width, height;
  7322   void (*surface_set_size_func) (cairo_surface_t *, double, double) = NULL;
  7323   Lisp_Object acc = Qnil;
  7324   specpdl_ref count = SPECPDL_INDEX ();
  7325 
  7326   specbind (Qredisplay_dont_pause, Qt);
  7327   redisplay_preserve_echo_area (31);
  7328 
  7329   f = XFRAME (XCAR (frames));
  7330   frames = XCDR (frames);
  7331   width = FRAME_PIXEL_WIDTH (f);
  7332   height = FRAME_PIXEL_HEIGHT (f);
  7333 
  7334   block_input ();
  7335 #ifdef CAIRO_HAS_PDF_SURFACE
  7336   if (surface_type == CAIRO_SURFACE_TYPE_PDF)
  7337     {
  7338       surface = cairo_pdf_surface_create_for_stream (pgtk_cr_accumulate_data, &acc,
  7339                                                      width, height);
  7340       surface_set_size_func = cairo_pdf_surface_set_size;
  7341     }
  7342   else
  7343 #endif
  7344 #ifdef CAIRO_HAS_PNG_FUNCTIONS
  7345   if (surface_type == CAIRO_SURFACE_TYPE_IMAGE)
  7346     surface = cairo_image_surface_create (CAIRO_FORMAT_RGB24, width, height);
  7347   else
  7348 #endif
  7349 #ifdef CAIRO_HAS_PS_SURFACE
  7350   if (surface_type == CAIRO_SURFACE_TYPE_PS)
  7351     {
  7352       surface = cairo_ps_surface_create_for_stream (pgtk_cr_accumulate_data, &acc,
  7353                                                     width, height);
  7354       surface_set_size_func = cairo_ps_surface_set_size;
  7355     }
  7356   else
  7357 #endif
  7358 #ifdef CAIRO_HAS_SVG_SURFACE
  7359   if (surface_type == CAIRO_SURFACE_TYPE_SVG)
  7360     surface = cairo_svg_surface_create_for_stream (pgtk_cr_accumulate_data, &acc,
  7361                                                    width, height);
  7362   else
  7363 #endif
  7364     abort ();
  7365 
  7366   cr = cairo_create (surface);
  7367   cairo_surface_destroy (surface);
  7368   record_unwind_protect_ptr (pgtk_cr_destroy, cr);
  7369 
  7370   while (1)
  7371     {
  7372       cairo_t *saved_cr = FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f);
  7373       FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f) = cr;
  7374       pgtk_clear_area (f, 0, 0, width, height);
  7375       expose_frame (f, 0, 0, width, height);
  7376       FRAME_CR_CONTEXT (f) = saved_cr;
  7377 
  7378       if (NILP (frames))
  7379         break;
  7380 
  7381       cairo_surface_show_page (surface);
  7382       f = XFRAME (XCAR (frames));
  7383       frames = XCDR (frames);
  7384       width = FRAME_PIXEL_WIDTH (f);
  7385       height = FRAME_PIXEL_HEIGHT (f);
  7386       if (surface_set_size_func)
  7387         (*surface_set_size_func) (surface, width, height);
  7388 
  7389       unblock_input ();
  7390       maybe_quit ();
  7391       block_input ();
  7392     }
  7393 
  7394 #ifdef CAIRO_HAS_PNG_FUNCTIONS
  7395   if (surface_type == CAIRO_SURFACE_TYPE_IMAGE)
  7396     {
  7397       cairo_surface_flush (surface);
  7398       cairo_surface_write_to_png_stream (surface, pgtk_cr_accumulate_data, &acc);
  7399     }
  7400 #endif
  7401   unblock_input ();
  7402 
  7403   unbind_to (count, Qnil);
  7404 
  7405   return CALLN (Fapply, intern ("concat"), Fnreverse (acc));
  7406 }
